
1a1(mdo 'grel): mgon po byams pas mdzad pa'i theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan bzhugs//
1b1(mdo 'grel): rgya gar skad du/ mahA yA na sU trA laM kA ra kA ri kA/ bod skad du/ theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan
1b2(mdo 'grel): gyi tshig le'ur byas pa/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ /don shes don ston
1b3(mdo 'grel): rab tu byed pa ngag dang tshig rnams dri med pas/ /sdug bsngal bsgral phyir sdug bsngal 'gro la snying rje'i phyir te de'i bdag nyid/
1b4(mdo 'grel): theg mchog bstan pa'i rnam pa chos kyi de yis 'gro ba'i sems can la/ /'byor pa'i don tshul bla med gyur pa lnga yi bdag nyid
2a1(mdo 'grel): ston par byed/ /gser las brdungs byas 'dra zhing pad+ma rgyas pa bzhin/ /bkres pas nyen pa g.yos
2a2(mdo 'grel): legs kha zas za ba 'dra/ /'phrin yig legs par thos 'dra rin chen sgrom phyi ltar/ /chos de 'dir bshad pas kyang dga' 
2a3(mdo 'grel): ba'i mchog bskyed do/ /gzugs rgyan rang bzhin yon tan ldan pa me long nang song ba/ /mthong ba'i dbang gis mi rnams rab tu
2a4(mdo 'grel): dga' bI mchog bskyed pa/ /de bzhin legs gsungs rtag tu rang bzhin yon tan ldan pa yi/ /chos kyang don rnams phye bas
2b1(mdo 'grel): mkhas rnams 'di na dga' mchog bskyed/ /ji ltar mnams na rab dku la/ /myangs na zhim pa'i sman bzhin du/ /de bzhin chos kyang gnyis
2b2(mdo 'grel): su gnas/ /don dang yi ger shes par bya/ /chos bka' rgya chen zab mo 'di/ /rgyal po bzhin du mnyes par dka' / /mnyes par byas
2b3(mdo 'grel): na de bzhin du/ /yon tan mchog gi nor sbyin byed/ /rin chen rigs ldan rin thang med/ /lta mi shes pa'i mi mi mgu /de bzhin mi mkhas
2b4(mdo 'grel): chos 'di la/ /bzlog na de bzhin mgu bar 'gyur/ /sngar lung ma bstan lhan cig byung/ /spyod yul ma yin grub pa dang/ /yod dang med na
2b5(mdo 'grel): yod med dang/ /gnyen po dang ni sgra gzhan phyir/ /sangs rgyas rnams ni mngon sum spyan/ /bstan pa dag kyang srung bar mdzad/ /dus
3a1(mdo 'grel): la'ang ye shes ma bsgribs pa/ /de phyir btang snyoms mi rung ngo/ /ma tshang ba dang 'gal ba dang/ /thabs min de ltar ma bstan phyir/ /nyan thos kyi
3a2(mdo 'grel): ni theg pa 'di/ /theg chen chos shes bya ba min/ /bsam pa dang ni bstan pa dang/ /sbyor ba dang ni rton pa dang/ /dus 'gal phyir na dman pa gang/ /de ni dman pa
3a3(mdo 'grel): kho na yin/ /rang gi nyid la 'jug pa dang/ /rang gi 'dul ba'ang snang phyir dang/ /zab pa'i phyir dang rgya che'i phyir/ /chos nyid dang ni 'gal ba med/ /rtog gi rten
3a4(mdo 'grel): cing ma nges la/ /ma khyab kun rdzob skyo ba can/ /byis pa la ni brten par 'dod/ /de phyir de ni de'i yul min/ /rgya che'i phyir dang zab pa'i phyir/ /yongs su smin
3a5(mdo 'grel): dang rnam mi rtog /de phyir 'di las gnyis bstan te/ /de ni bla na med pa'i thabs/ /'gro ba de'i gnas min la skrag pas gdung byed 'gyur/ /bsod nams ma yin
3b1(mdo 'grel): phung byed bsags byas yun ring du/ /rigs ngan grogs ngan sngon dge ma bsags blo ma sbyangs/ /chos 'dis skrag 'gyur 'di ni don chen 'di las ltung/ /de las gzhan dang gzhan med shin tu zab cing
3b2(mdo 'grel): rjes song phyir/ /sna tshogs ston cing mang po'i sgo nas rtag tu ston dang ldan/ /ji skad bshad bzhin don min bcom ldan dgongs pa shin tu zab/ /mkhas pa rnams kyis tshul bzhin brtags na chos 'dir
3b3(mdo 'grel): skrag mi 'gyur/ /'di na dang por thos la brten nas yid la byed pa 'byung/ /tshul bzhin yid la byed las yang dag don yul ye shes 'byung/ /de las chos thob de yod de las blo gros
3b4(mdo 'grel): rab tu skye/ /gang tshe de ni so so rang rig med na ji ltar nges/ /bdag gis mi shes sangs rgyas zab mo mkhyen ma yin/ /zab mo tsa yi phyir na rtog gi'i yul ma yin/ /ci phyir zab mo'i don rig pa dag
3b5(mdo 'grel): mthar 'gyur zhes/ /bya ba de ni skrag pa'i gnas su rigs ma yin/ /dman par mos shing khams kyang shin tu dman/ /grogs po dman pa dag gis yongs bskor ba/ /zab cing rgya che legs
3b6(mdo 'grel): par bshad pa'i chos/ /'di la gal te mos med grub pa yin/ /thos rjes 'brangs te blo ldan thob nas ni/ /gang zhig thos la rab tu brnyas byed pa/ /rnam pa sna tshogs dpag tu med lus la/ /
4a1(mdo 'grel): rmongs pa gang gi phyir na nges par byed/ /don sgra ji bzhin yongs rtog na/ /bdag nyid bsnyems shing blo nyams 'gyur/ /legs par gsungs pa'ang spangs pas na/ /brlag 'gyur chos la khong
4a2(mdo 'grel): khros sgrib/ /yid kyi nyes pa rang bzhin gdug pa ste/ /ma rigs pa'i gzugs la'ang ma rigs na/ /the tshom za ba'i chos la smos ci dgos/ /de phyir btang snyoms bzhag legs nyes ba med/ /sgrub pa'i skabs
4a3(mdo 'grel): rdzogs so// //kun tu 'gro dang khas len rtogs dang zil gnon par/ /dbye ba'i rang bzhin don rnams bzhi yi khyad par gyis/ /theg pa mchog phyir dkon mchog skyabs rab song ba gang/ /de nyid skyabs
4a4(mdo 'grel): su song ba rnams kyi mchog ces bya/ /gang phyir dang por nges par bya ba 'di dka' ste/ /de ni bskal pa stong phrag du mar sgrub bar dka' / /gang phyir grub na sems can phan byed don chen te/ /de phyir theg chen 'di la skyabs
4a5(mdo 'grel): don mchog yin no/ /gang zhig sems can thams cad bsgral bar zhugs pa dang/ theg pa ye shes kun tu 'gro la mkhas par ldan/ /gang zhig mya ngan 'das la 'khor zhi ro gcig pa/ /de 'dra'i blo
4a6(mdo 'grel): ldan de 'dir kun 'gro shes par bya/ /gang zhig dga' ba mang pos byang chub mchog don gnyer/ /gang zhig skyo ba med par dka' ba yang dag spyod/ /gang zhig rnam sangs rgyas nas sangs rgyas kun mnyam 'gyur/ /blo ldan de ni mkhas
4b1(mdo 'grel): khas len mchog tu shes bar bya/ sangs rgyas sras kyi mchog tu legs par gang skyes pa/ /sems dang shes rab dang ni tshogs ldan snying rje 'di'i/ /sa bon ma dang mngal gnas ma ma mtshungs pa med/ /blo ldan de ni khas len mchog tu shes par bya/ /sna tshogs mtshan rnams kun gyis de lus
4b2(mdo 'grel): rgyan/ /sems can thams cad smin par byed stobs thob/ /sangs rgyas bde chen mdza' yas zhi brnyed/ /sems can kun bskyab thabs chen bshams pa shes/ /sangs rgyas kun gyis 'od zer chen pos dbang bskur byin/ /de ni chos la dbang ba kun dang yang dag ldan/ /sangs rgyas
4b3(mdo 'grel): 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor ston pa'i rnam par shes/ /bslab pa bca' bas tshar bcad phan 'dogs byed la brtson/ /blon po chen po lta bur pha rol phyin la 'jug ba'i phyir/ /byang chub chen po phyogs mthun bdal? la rtag tu spyan byed phyir/ /gsang ba'i gnas ni rnam gsum yang
4b4(mdo 'grel): dag rtag tu 'dzin pa'i phyir/ /sems can mang don rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par rab byed phyir/ /bsod nams phung chen srid gsum bla ma srid ba'i bde ba dang/ /sdug bsngal phung po chen po rab zhi blo mchog bde ba dang/ /chos mang po mchog rab rtag pa'i sku ste dge ba'i tshogs/ /bag
4b5(mdo 'grel): chags bzlog cing srid dang zhi las rnam par grol ba 'thob/ /blo ldan nyan thos tshogs bcas dge ba rgya chen don che dang/ /mdza' yas rtag rgyun mi 'chad zad mi shes pas zil gyi gnon/ /dge ba de yang 'jig rten 'jig rten ma yin yongs smin byed/ dbang 'byor rnyed pa de ni
4b6(mdo 'grel): phung bo zhi bas? dang? mi shes/ /'di ni de dngos 'dod pas khas len de yang snying brtse las rig bya/ /de las rnam pa kun mkhyen phan dang? bde byed bka' la skye ba med/ /nges par 'byung la theg pa kun gyis brten ba'i yon tan rtag tu ldan/ /brda dang chos nyid thob pa blo ldan rnams kyi
4b7(mdo 'grel): skyabs 'gro 'di mchog yin/ /skyabs su 'gro ba 'dir song don chen te/ /des ni tshad med yon tan tshogs 'phel 'gyur/ /'gro ba 'di la snying rje'i bsam pas khyab/ /tshungs med 'phags chen kyang rgyas bar byed/ /skabs su 'gro ba'i skabs rdzogs so// // 
5a1(mdo 'grel): yod dang mchog dang mtshan nyid dang/ /rtags dang rigs rab dbye ba dang/ /nyes dmigs dang ni phan yon dang/ /dpe rnam gnyis te rnam pa bzhi/ /khams rnams dang ni mos pa dang/ /sgrub pa tha dad dbye ba dang/ /'bras bu tha dad dmigs pa'i phyir/ /rigs yod
5a2(mdo 'grel): nyid du nges par brjod/ /de dag khyad par 'phags pa dang/ /thams cad dang ni don chen dang/ /mi zad pa yi rgyu mtshan phyir/ /rigs mchog nyid ces brjod pa yin/ /rang bzhin dang ni rgyas pa dang/ /de ni rten dang brten pa dang/ /yod med nyid dang yon tan dang/ /sgrol ba'i
5a3(mdo 'grel): don du shes par bya/ /sbyor ba'i sngon du snying rje dang/ /mos ba dang ni bzod pa dang/ /dge ba yang dag sbyong ba ni/ /rigs kyis rtags su nges par bshad/ /rigs ni nges dang ma nges pa/ /rkyen rnams kyis ni mi 'phrogs dang/ /'phrogs pa nyid de mdor na rigs/ /dbye ba de ni
5a4(mdo 'grel): rnam pa bzhi/ nyon mongs goms dang grogs ngan dang/ /phongs dang gzhan gyi dbang nyid de/ /mdor na rigs kyi nyes dmigs dag/ rnam pa gzhir ni shes bar bya/ /ring mo zhig nas ngan song du/ /'gro zhing myur du thar pa dang/ /de na'ang sdug bsngal chung du myong/ /skye bcas
5a5(mdo 'grel): sems can smin par byed/ /gser gyi rigs bzhin shes par bya/ /dge ba dpag tu med pa'i gnas/ /ye shes dang ni dri med ldan/ /mthu rnams kyi yang gnas yin no/ /rin chen mchog rigs bzhin shes bya ? byang chub chen po'i rgyu mtshan phyir/ /ye shes che dang ting
5a6(mdo 'grel): 'dzin 'phags/ /sems can mang po'i don gnas phyir/ /la la gcig tu nyes par spyod nges yod/ /la la dkar po'i chos rnams kun tu bcom/ /la la thar pa'i cha mthun dge ba med/ /dkar po dman pa yod pa rgyu dang bral/ /zab cing rgya cher bshad pa gzhan la
5a7(mdo 'grel): phan phyir bstan pa'i chos chen la/ /mi shes bzhin du mos pa shin tu rgya chen 'byung bzhin sgrub la bzod/ /de dag tha mar rnam pa gnyis mchog phun sum tshogs 'gyur gang yin de/ /byang chub sems dpa' rang bzhin yon ldan de rgyas ba'i rigs las shes//
5b1(mdo 'grel): yon tan shin tu rgya che byang chub shing bskyed phyir/ /bde dang sdug bsngal chen po zhi ba thob bya'i phyir/ /bdag dang gzhan la phan bde byed pa 'bras bu'i phyir/ /rigs mchog de ni rtsa ba bzang po lta bu yin/ /rigs kyi skabs rdzogs so// //spro ba che dang rtsom pa che/ /don che ba dang
5b2(mdo 'grel): 'byung ba che/ /byang chub sems dpa' i sems pa ste/ /don gnyis ldan pa'i sems 'byung ba/ /sems bskyed de ni sa rnams la/ /mos dang lhag bsam dag pa dang/ /rnam par smin pa gzhan du 'dod/ /de bzhin sgrib pa spangs pa'o/ /de yi rtsa ba snying rjer 'dod/ /rtag tu sems can phan par
5b3(mdo 'grel): sems/ /chos la mos dang de bzhin de'i/ /ye shes tshol bar dmigs pa'o/ /gong du 'dun pa 'gro ba ste/ /sdom pa rgya chen de yi rten/ /lam 'gog pa ni mi mthun phyogs/ /slong zhing dang du len pa'o/ /bsod nams ye shes rang bzhin gyi/ /dge ba 'phel ba de phan yon/ /pha rol phyin
5b4(mdo 'grel): la rtag sbyor ba/ /de ni nges par 'byung bar brjod/ /'di yi mthar thug pa yin te/ /so so rang gi de sbyor bas/ /byang chub sems dpa' i sems bskyed pa/ /rnam par nges par shes par bya/ /grogs stobs rgyu stobs rtsa ba'i stobs/ /thos stobs dge ba goms pa la/ /mi brtan
5b5(mdo 'grel): pa dang brtan 'byung ba/ /gzhan gyi bstan pa'i sems bskyed bshad/ /rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rab bsnyen byas/ /bsod nams ye shes tshogs rab bsags/ /chos la mi rtog ye shes ni/ /skyes phyir de ni dam par 'dod/ /chos dang sems can rnams dang ni/ /de yi bya ba
5b6(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas nyid/ /mchog la sems mnyam rnyed pa'i phyir/ /de yi rab dga' khyad par 'phags/ /skye ba rgya che de la spro/ /bsam pa yang ni dag pa dang/ /lhag ma dag la mkhas pa dang/ /nges par 'byung ba shes par bya/ /chos la mos pa sa bon dang/ /pha rol phyin mchog ma
5b7(mdo 'grel): las skyes bsam gtan las byung bde ba mngal/ /snying rje bskyed pa'i ma ma'o/ /smon lam chen po bcu sgrub phyir/ /rgya che bar ni shes bar bya/ /dka' ba yun ring mi skyo phyir/ /spro ba khong du chung bar bya/ /byang chub nye bar rtogs pa dang/ /de yi thabs shes rnyed pa'i
6a1(mdo 'grel): phyir/ bsam ba dag par shes par bya/ /sa gzhan tshul la mkhas pa nyid/ /ji ltar rnam gzhag yid byed pas/ /de rtog nyid du shes phyir dang/ /de nyid la yang mi rtog phyir/ /nges par 'gyur bar shes bar bya/ /bskyed pa sa dang mtshungs pa ste/ /gzhan ni
6a2(mdo 'grel): bzang po'i gser dang 'dra/ /zla ba yar gyi chos pa bzhin/ /gzhan ni ma dang 'dra shes bya/ /gzhan ni gter chen bzhin shes bya/ /gzhan ni rin chen 'byung gnas bzhin/ /rgya mtsho 'dra bar shes bya gzhan/ /rdo rje dang 'dra ri rab 'dra/ /sman gyi rgyal po 'dra pa ste//
6a3(mdo 'grel): gzhan ni 'dza' chen 'drar shes bya/ /yid bzhin nor bu 'dra ba dang/ /gzhan ni nyi ma 'drar shes bya/ /gzhan ni dri za'i dbyangs snyan bzhin/ /gzhan ni rgyal po 'dra shes bya/ /de bzhin gzhan ni mdzod lta bu/ /lam po che dang 'drar shes bya/ /theg pa 'drar shes
6a4(mdo 'grel): gzhan ni 'dza' chen 'drar shes bya/ /yid bzhin nor bu 'dra ba dang/ /gzhan ni nyi ma 'drar shes bya/ /gzhan ni dri za'i dbyangs snyan bzhin/ /gzhan ni rgyal po 'dra shes bya/ /de bzhin gzhan ni mdzod lta bu/ /lam po che dang 'drar shes bya/ /theg pa 'drar shes
6a5(mdo 'grel): bya ba ste/ /sems bskyed bkod ma 'dra ba yin/ /kun dga' i sgra dang 'dra ba ste/ /klung chen rgyun dang 'dra ba'o/ /rgyal sras rnams kyis sems bskyed pa/ /sprin dang 'dra bar bstan pa ste/ /de phyir de ltar yon tan phyug/ sems ni dga' bas yang dag bskyed
6a6(mdo 'grel): ched 'os sems bskyed spangs pa'i skye bo dag/ gzhan don sems dang de yi thabs rnyed dang/ /dgongs chen don dang de ny+d mchog mthong ba'i/ /bde ba de spangs zhi bar 'gro bar 'gyur/ /blo ldan sems mchog bskyed ma thag tu yang/ /mdza' yas nyes pa byed
6a7(mdo 'grel): las sems rab bsdams/ /gnyis 'phel byed pas rtag tu dge ba dang/ /brtse ldan bde dang sdug bsngal dag gis dga' / /gang tshe gzhan gyi don phyir lus dang ni/ /srog la mi lta rab mngal khas len pa/ /de lta bu de gzhan gyi gnod pa yis/ /ji ltar ngan pa byed
6a8(mdo 'grel): pa'i las la 'jug /de yis chos kun sgyu ma lta bu dang/ /skye ba skye mos tshal 'gro ltar rtogs nas/ /'byor pa'i dus dang rgud pa'i dus na'ang 'di/ /nyon mongs sdug bsngal dag gis 'jigs pa med/ /rang gis yon tan sems can phan 'dogs dga' //?
6b1(mdo 'grel): bzhin skye ba rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul/ /rgyan dang ston mo mchogs? rtse dga' ba/ /snying rje'i bdag nyid min pa rnams la med/ /gzhan don brtson ldan snying rje'i bdag nyid 'di/ /gang tshe mnar med pa la'ang dgar 'dzin pa/ /de 'dra ba dag srid na gzhan brten can/ /sdug bsngal 'byung
6b2(mdo 'grel): ba rnams kyis ga la 'jigs/ /slob dpon brtse chen rtag tu brten pa'i bdag/ pha rol sdug bsngal dag gis sems gdung ba/ /gzhan gyi bya ba nye bar gnas pa la/ /gzhan gyis bskul ba shin tu ngo tsha yang/ /mgo la sems can khur chen khyer ba yi/ /sems can mchog
6b3(mdo 'grel): ni dal gyis 'gro mi mdzes/ /bdag gzhan sna tshogs 'ching bas rab bcings ba/ /brtson 'grus brgya 'gyur du ni bya ba'i rigs/ /sems bskyed ba'i skabs rdzogs so// //gnas rtsom 'bras bu 'byung ba che bdag nyid/ /rgyal sras rnams kyi sgrub pa yin par
6b4(mdo 'grel): 'dod/ /rtag tu len pa che dang bzod pa che/ /don chen yang dag sgrub pa'i bya ba byed/ /gzhan dang bdag tu snyam pa'i sems nyid dam/ /bdag pas gzhan chos sdug pa snyed nas ni/ /de ltar bdag pas gzhan don mchog tu shes/ /rang gi don gang gzhan gyi don gang yin de
6b5(mdo 'grel): ltar snying rje'i bdag nyid gzhan gyi don gyi phyir/ /bdag gi sdug bsngal sna tshogs gdung bar rab byed pa/ /de ltar 'jig rten gdung ba'i las kyi gzhan dgra la/ /shin tu brtse ba med par rab tu 'jug pa ma yin/ /tha chad 'bring dang mchog chos nyid gnas la/ /legs par
6b6(mdo 'grel): ston dang mgru byed 'jug pa dang/ /don la rnam nges dge ba yongs smin byed/ /de bzhin gdams ngag gnas dang blo rnam grol/ /yon tan khyad par can 'grub de bzhin du/ /rigs su skye dang lung bstan dbang bskur dang/ /de bzhin gshegs mkhyen bla med go 'phang ste//
6b7(mdo 'grel): bcu gsum bdag nyid 'di ni? gzhan gyi don/ /skye bo dang mthun phyin ci ma log 'chad/ /mi 'gying ba dang bdag gi med la mkhas/ /bzod du la shin tu ring song mi bzod pa/ /rgyal sras rnams kyi sgrub pa mchog yin no/ /'dod ldan skye ba 'jigs pa che la 'jug
7a1(mdo 'grel): srid dga' phyir ci log bde g.yo ba la/ /zhi dga' rang gi len pa rab zhil/ /snying rje'i bdag nyid len kun zhi la rtag/ skye bo rmongs ba rang gi bde don brtsom/ rtag tu de ma thog pa sdug bsngal 'gyur/ /brten pa rtag tu gzhan don brtson ldan pa/ /gnyis
7a2(mdo 'grel): ga'i don byas mya ngan 'da' bar 'gyur/ /rgyal sras sbyod tshe ji lta ji lta bur/ /dbang po'i spyod yul sna tshogs 'jug par 'gyur/ /de lta de ltar rigs pa mthun tshig gis/ /sems can don phyir de mngon 'du byed do/ /rtag tu nyes pas rang dbang med par byas
7a3(mdo 'grel): sems kyi/ /skye bo la ni blo ldan nyes par mi 'dzin te/ /mi 'dod bzhin du log par sgrub par 'gyur ro zhes/ /skye bo dag la snying rje rnam par 'phel phyir ro/ /sgrub pa 'dis ni srid dang 'gro ba kun/ /zil gyis gnan 'gro zhi ba mchog dang ldan/ /yon tan sna tshogs
7a4(mdo 'grel): dag gis rnam par 'phel/ /byams pa'i bsam pas rtag tu 'gro ba sdu/ /sgrub pa'i skabs rdzogs so// //yod min med min de bzhin min gzhan min/ /skyed dang 'jig med 'bri bar mi 'gyur te/ /'phel ba med cing rnam par dag pa'ang med/ /rnam
7a5(mdo 'grel): par dag 'gyur de ni don dam mtshan/ /bdag tu lta ba bdag nyid bdag mtshan mig ngan par gnas min mtshan nyid mi 'dra phyir/ /gnyis las gzhan med de ni nor pa skyes/ /de phyir thar pa nor tsam zad pa yin/ /ji ltar 'khrul pa tsam brten skye bo yis/ /sdug bsngal
7a6(mdo 'grel): rang bzhin rgyun chags rtogs mi 'gyur/ /rig min rig nyid sdug bsngal sdug bsngal med/ /chos kyi rang bzhin de yi rang bzhin min/ /brten nas dngos rab skye bar mngon 'jug na/ /skye ba ji ltar gzhan gyis byas la brten/ /gang phyir yod pa mi mthong med pa
7a7(mdo 'grel): mthong/ /'di 'dra'i mun nag rnam pa de gang zhi lta 'di la don dam tshul gyis zhi ba dang/ /skye ba de gnyis khyad par ci yang med/ /'on kyang dge ba'i las rnams byed pa dag/ skye ba zad pas zhib thob bar bshad/ /byang chub sems dpas bsod nams ye shes kyi/ /mdza' 
7b1(mdo 'grel): yas pha rol tshogs rnams legs bsags nas/ /chos la sems pa shin tu rnam nges phyir/ /don gyi rnam pa brjod pa'i rgyu can rtogs/ /de yis brjod ba tsam du don rig nas/ /der snang sems tsam la ni yang dag gnas/ /de nas chos dbyings gnyis kyi mtshan nyid dang/
7b2(mdo 'grel): bral bas mngon sum nyid du rtogs par 'gyur/ /sems las gzhan med par ni blos rig nas/ /de nas sems kyang med pa nyid du rtogs/ /blo dang ldan pas gnyis po med rig nas/ /de mi ldan pa'i chos kyi dbyings la gnas/ /blo dang ldan pa mi rtogs ye shes stobs//
7b3(mdo 'grel): rtag tu kun nas mnyam par song ba yis/ /de la brten pa'i nyes tshogs tshang ching dag/ dug sman chen pos dug bzhin sel bar byed/ /thub pas gsungs pa'i dam chos legs bzhag pa/ /rtsa ba chos kyi dbyings la blo gros bzhag/ dran rgyu rtogs pa tsam rigs brtan pa
7b4(mdo 'grel): dag/ myur du yon tan rgya mtsho'i pha rol 'gro/ de kho na nyid kyi skabs rdzogs so// //skye dang ngag sems dge dang mi dge bskyed/ /de yi gnas dang nges 'byung mngon sum gang/ /shes pa kun 'gro rab tu dbye bcas la/ /thog med brtan pa thob pa'i mthu yin no/ /bsam gtan
7b5(mdo 'grel): bzhi ba shin tu dag thob nas/ /mi rtog ye shes yongs su bzung ba dang/ /ji ltar rnam gnas yid la byed pa las/ /mthu grub pa yi dam pa thob par 'gyur/ /gang gis 'phags dang lha dang tshangs pa yis/ /gnas pa dpe med rgya ches rtag tu gnas/ /phyogs su de song sangs rgyas
7b6(mdo 'grel): sems can dag/ /yang dag mchod byed rnam par dag pa bskyed/ /chags dang 'jig bcas sems can bcas pa yi/ /'jig rten khams rnams sgyu ma lta bur mthong/ /dbang ldan ji ltar 'dod bzhin de dag dang/ /rnam bcas sna tshogs dag kyang yang dag ston/ /'od zer btang
7b7(mdo 'grel): bas shin tu sdug bsngal ba'i/ /ngan song bdag mtho ris 'gro bar byed/ /bdud gnas gzhal med khang mtho mdzes pa dag/ bdud bcas kun tu bskyod cing sgrag? bar byed/ /de ni mchog tshogs nang du ting nge 'dzin/ /dpag med rnam par rol pa kun ston zhing/ /las dang skye dang
8a1(mdo 'grel): mchog gi sprul pa yi/ /sems can rnams kyi don du dus kun gnas/ /ye shes dag la dbang phyir zhing rnams ni/ /ji ltar 'dod bzhin bstan phyir ngag pa thob/ /sangs rgyas mtshan mi grags bar sangs rgyas mtshan/ /yang dag bsgrags pas de dag khams
8a2(mdo 'grel): gzhan 'gyed/ /'dab gshog kun tu rgyas pa'i bya bzhin du/ /sems can smin par byed par nus pa nyid/ /sangs rgyas las ni shin tu bsngags pa 'thob/ /skye dgu rnams la tshig bzung 'os par 'gyur/ /mngon par shes pa drug dang rig pa gsum rnam thar brgyad
8a3(mdo 'grel): dang de bzhin zil gnon brgyad/ /zad par skye mched bcu dang ting nge 'dzin/ /dpag tu med pa brtan pa thob pa'i mthu/ /de ni dbang mchog thob pa'i blo dang ldan/ /'gro ba dbang med rang dbang bkod rtag tu/ /gzhan la phan bya gcig tu mngon dga' ste/ /seng ge bzhan du rab brtan
8a4(mdo 'grel): srid na spyod/ /mthu'i skabs rdzogs so// //dga' dang dang dang rab zhi snying rje dang/ /bzod dang yid gzhungs mthu can nyid dang ni/ /mi 'phrogs pa dang yan lag ldan pa rag/ de ni rgyal sras yongs su smin pa'i mtshan/ /grogs mchog la sogs gsum dang brtson rab dang
8a5(mdo 'grel): mthar phyin dam pa dang ni chos mchog sdud/ /dam chos cher bzung phyir ni snying rje can/ /yang dag yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid 'dod/ /yon tan shes dang sems kyang mi phyed dang/ /ting 'dzin myur du thob dang 'bras bu myong/ /ston la yid ches bya phyir rgyal sras kyi/ /yang dag
8a6(mdo 'grel): yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid 'dod/ /shin tu sdom zhing nyon mongs rtog pa spong/ /bar chad med cing dge la mngon par dga' / /rgyal ba'i sras kyi nyon mongs bsal ba'i phyir/ /yang dag yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid 'dod/ /rang bzhin snying brtse gzhan gyi sdug bsngal
8a7(mdo 'grel): mthong/ /dman pa'i sems kyang yang dag rab tu spong/ /khyad par 'gro dang 'gro ba'i mchog gyur lus/ /gzhan la snying brtse yongs su smin pa'i mtshan/ /rang bzhin brtan pa so sor brtags bsgom pa/ /grang sogs sdug bsngal shin tu rtag mi 'byed/ /khyad par 'gro dang
8b1(mdo 'grel): dag la mngon par dga' / bzod pa yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid 'dod/ /rnam smin dag cing thos sogs dran mi brjed/ /de bzhin legs bshad nyes par smras pa dag/ shes rab blo chen skye bar rung ba nyid/ /shin tu yid gzhungs yongs su smin pa'i mtshan/ /dge ba gnyis kyi khams
8b2(mdo 'grel): gnyis brtas pa dang/ /rten ni 'bras bu skye bar rung ba'i mchog/ yid la bsam 'grub 'gro ba'i mchog gyur pa/ /mthu thob yongs su smin ba'i mtshan nyid do/ /chos bzang rigs pas rnam dpyad bsam pa can/ /rtag tu bdud kyis bar chad byed pa med/ /khyad par rnyed dang gzhan
8b3(mdo 'grel): gyi phyogs su na 'byin/ /mi 'phrogs yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid do/ /dge ba bsags dang rten kyang brtson par rung/ /dben dang dge ba mchog la mngon dga' ba/ /rgyal ba sras kyi yan lag ldan pa yi/ /yang dag yongs su smin pa'i mtshan nyid do/ /de ltar dngos po rnam
8b4(mdo 'grel): dgus smin pa'i bdag/ pha rol yongs su smin byed rung dang ldan/ /chos kyi rang bzhin rgyun 'phel bdag nyid can/ /rtag tu 'gro ba'i gnyen mchog gyur pa yin/ /ji ltar rma dang zas la de dag gi /gzag? dang spyad du rung ba smin 'dod ltar/ /de bzhin rten 'dir phyogs gnyis zhib
8b5(mdo 'grel): dang/ /de bzhin spyod pa nyid du smin pa bstan/ /lus can bral bar smin byed de bzhin du/ /yongs smin rab smin mthun par smin nbyed gzhan/ /legs par smin byed rtogs pa smin byed dang/ /rtag min gong du smin byed bshad par 'dod/ /ji ltar rgyal sras phan pa'i bsam pas
8b6(mdo 'grel): 'dir/ /'gro kun rnam par smin byed gnas pa ltar/ /de bzhin pha dang ma dang gnyen bshes rnams/ /bu dang gnyen pa rnams la legs mi gnas/ /ji ltar brtse bdag bde dang phan sbyor phyir/ /sems can gzhan la byams 'dod de ltar ni/ /skye bo bdag la byams par
8b7(mdo 'grel): mi 'dod na/ /rab sdug skyo bo gzhan rten smos ci dgos/ /byang chub sems dpa' i lus dang longs spyod dag/ gzhan la mi sbyin pa ni yod med de/ /phan 'dogs rnam pa gnyis kyis gzhan smin byed/ /mnyam par sbyin pa'i yon tan ngoms mi 'gyur ro/ /rtag pa rang bzhin 
9a1(mdo 'grel): lhag par 'tshe ba med/ /bdag dga' bag yod 'di la gzhan 'god cing/ /phan rnam gnyis 'dogs rnam par smin pa dang/ /rgyu mthun yon tan rgyud pas gzhan smin byed/ /gzhan gnod byed la phan byed blo ldan pa/ /gnod byed drag po
9a2(mdo 'grel): dag kyang rab tu bzod/ /thabs rigs gnod byed bzod pa de dag gis/ /gnod byed dge ba yang dag len du 'jug /rgyal sras brtson 'grus mchog la brten pa ste/ /sems can tshogs rab smin par byed pa na/ /pha rol sems dge gcig gi phyir yang
9a3(mdo 'grel): ni/ /bskal pa bye ba stong du 'ang skyo mi 'gyur/ /yid kyi dbang ni bla na med thob nas/ /gzhan gyi mchod pa thams cad nges bcom ste/ /mchog gi bstan la gzhan dag 'dun byed cing/ /de dag dge bas yang dag 'phel bar byed/ /de nyid dgongs
9a4(mdo 'grel): don tshul la rab nges te/ /sems can the tshom shin tu sel bar byed/ /de phyir rgyal ba'i bstan la de gus pas/ /rang bzhin dge ba'i yon tan rnam 'phel byed/ /de ltar byang chub sems dpa' i snying rje yis/ /'gro kun bde 'gro'i 'gro ba'am dge gsum
9a5(mdo 'grel): la/ /rnam pa chung dang mchog dang 'bring dag gis/ /'jig rten yod dang mnyam par 'jug pas 'dul/ /yongs su smin pa'i skabs rdzogs so// //dka' spyod dpag med brgya phrag dang/ /dpag med dge ba bsags pa dang/ /dpag tu med
9a6(mdo 'grel): pa'i dus dpag med sgrib pa zad pa'i phyir/ /sgrib pa kun gyi dri med pa/ /rnam pa thams cad mkhyen nyid thob/ /rin chen snod ni bya ba ltar/ /sangs rgyas nyid ni yang dag bstan/ /ngal rgyas rmad byung dka' spyad dge kun bsags/ /bskal mchog dus ring 'gro
9a7(mdo 'grel): ba'i sgrib kun zad/ /sar gtogs sgrib pa phra bcom sangs rgyas te/ /de ni mthu che rin chen snod phye bzhin/ /chos rnams thams cad sangs rgyas nyid/ /chos ni gang yang yod ma yin/ /de ni chos dkar rang bzhin yang/ /de yis de ni brjod ma yin/ /
9b1(mdo 'grel): rin chen chos kyi rgyu mtshan phyir/ /de ni rin chen 'byung gnas bzhin/ /dge ba'i lo tog rgyu mtshan phyir/ /de ni sprin dang 'dra bar 'dod/ /sangs rgyas nyid ni chos kun ldan pa'am yang na chos kun bral ba ste/ /rin chen chos rab che yangs 'byung phyir rin? chen? chos kyi 'byung ngas bzhin/ /skye
9b2(mdo 'grel): dgu rnams la legs bshad mi zad chos kyi char chen 'bebs pas na/ /'byung po'i me tog dkar po shin tu che 'phel rgyu phyir sprin dang 'dra /rtag tu nyon mongs tshogs kun dang/ /nyes par spyod pa thams cad dang/ /rga dang 'chi ba dag las kyang/ /sangs rgyas nyid ni yongs su
9b3(mdo 'grel): skyob/ /'tshe bdag ni thams cad dang/ /ngan song dang ni thabs min dang/ /'jigs tshogs theg pa dman pa las/ /de phyir skyabs kyi dam pa'o/ /sangs rgyas nyid de skyabs ni dpe med mchog tu 'dod/ /sna tshogs 'jigs gyur 'jigs tshogs kun dang theg pa dang/ /ngan song
9b4(mdo 'grel): rnam mang sdug bsngal thabs min song ba rnams/ /skye dang 'chi ba nyon mongs las rnams kun las srung/ /sangs rgyas chos kyi shin tu rdzogs pa'i sku gang yin/ /dam pa'i chos la semS can rab gdul mkhyen pa gang/ /'gro ba kun la thugs brtses pha rol phyin pa gang//
9b5(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas nyid de 'dir ni skyabs kyi mchog tu 'dod/ /'jig rten ji srid sems can gyi/ /gnod dang phun sum tshogs pa kun/ /bzlog cing 'byor par bya ba'i phyir/ /sangs rgyas skyabs chen nyid du 'dod/ /gang la nyon mongs shes bya'i sgrib pa'i sa bon dus ring rtag ldan
9b6(mdo 'grel): pa/ /spong pa shin tu rgya chen rnam pa kun gyis rab tu bcom gyur zhing/ /gnas gyur chos dkar yon tan mchog rab ldan pa thob pa sangs rgyas nyid/ /de ni mi rtog rab dag shin tu yul chen ye shes lam gyis thob/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de ni der bzhugs nas/ ri dbang
9b7(mdo 'grel): mtho steng bzhugs bzhin 'gro la gzigs/ /zhi bar mngon dga' i 'grol 'ang thugs rje na/ /srid la mngon dga' i skye bo gzhan ci smos/ /gnas la 'jug dang rab 'jug mi 'jug dang/ /ldog dang kun 'jug gnyis dang mi gnyis dang/ /mnyam dang khyad 'phags
10a1(mdo 'grel): kun 'gro'i bdag nyid ni/ /de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi yongs gyur 'dod/ /ji ltar nam mkha' rtag tu kun song?  'dod/ /de bzhin de yang rtag tu kun song 'dod/ /ji ltar nam mkha' gzuD gyur kun tu song/ /de bzhin de yang seMs can tshogS kun song/ ji ltar chu? yi snod chag
10a2(mdo 'grel): na/ zla ba'i gzugs brnyan mi snang ba/ /de bzhin sems can ngan pa la/ /sangs rgyas gzugs kyang mi snang ngo/ /ji ltar me ni gzhan du 'bar/ /gzhan du zhi bar gyur pa ltar/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas rnams la yang/ /snang dang mi snang shes par bya/ /ji ltar rnga dag ma brdungs par
10a3(mdo 'grel): sgra ni kun tu 'byung ba ltar/ /de bzhin rgyal ba bzod med par/ /bshad pa dag ni kun tu 'byung/ /ji ltar nor bu 'bad med par/ /rang gi 'ong ni ston ba ltar/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyang bzo med par/ /de bzhin mdzad pa nges par ston/ /ji ltar mkha' la 'jig rten gyi/ /bya ba
10a4(mdo 'grel): rgyun mi 'chad par snang/ /de bzhin zag med dbyings na yang/ /rgyal ba'i mdzad pa rgyun mi 'chad/ /ji ltar mkha' la rtag tu ni/ /bya ba nyams shing 'byung ba ltar/ /de bzhin zag med dbyings na yang/ /sangs rgyas phrin las skye zhing 'bri/ /snga ma phyi mar khyad med kyang//
10a5(mdo 'grel): sgrib ba kun gyi dri med pa/ /de bzhin nyid ni sangs rgyas 'dod/ /dag pa ma yin ma dag min/ /stong pa nyid ni rnam dag na/ /bdag med mchog gi bdag thob pas/ /sangs rgyas dag pa'i bdag thob phyir/ /bdag nyid chen po'i bdag tu 'gyur/ /de phyir sangs rgyas yod
10a6(mdo 'grel): min zhing/ /med par yang ni mi brjod do/ /de ltar sangs rgyas de skad 'dri/ /lung ma bstan pa'i tshul du 'dod/ /ji ltar lcaD la tsha ba dang/ /mig la rab rig zhi ba ltar/ /sangs rgyas sems dang ye shes la/ /yong dang med par mi brjod do/ /zag med dbyings na sangs rgyas
10a7(mdo 'grel): rnams/ /mkha' ltar lus ni med byir dang/ /sngon gyi lus rdzes? 'brang ba'i phyir/ /gcig min mang po nyid ma yin/ /stobs so/ /sangs rgyas chos rnams la/ /byang chub rin chen 'byung gnas 'dra/ /'gro ba'i dge ba'i li tog la/ /sprin chen dang yang 'dra bar 'dod/ bsod
10b1(mdo 'grel): nams ye shes rab rdzogs byir/ zla ba nya ba lta bur 'dod/ /ye shes snang ba byed pa'i phyir/ /nyi ma chen po 'dra bar 'dod/ /ji ltar nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gyis/ /'od zer dpag tu med 'dres shing/ /rtag tu bya ba gcig la 'jug /'jig rten la yang snang bar byed/ /de bzhin zag med dbyings na yang/ /
10b2(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas dpag tu med 'dres shig /mdzad pa gcig ni mdzad pa la/ /ye shes snang ba mdzad par 'dod/ /dper na nyi ma'i 'od zer gcig /byung na 'od zer kun 'byung ltar/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas rnams kyi yang/ /ye shes 'byung bar shes par bya/ /ji ltar nyi ma'i 'od zer dag /'jug la bdag
10b3(mdo 'grel): gir bya ba med/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas ye shes kyang/ /'jug la bdag gir mdzad mi mnga' / /nyi ma'i 'od zer gcig btang baS/ /'gro ba snang bar byed pa ltar/ /de bzhin shes bya thams cad la/ /sangs rgyas ye shes cig car snang/ /ji ltar nyi ma'i 'od zer rnams/ /sprin la sogs pas
10b4(mdo 'grel): bsgribs par 'dod/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas ye shes rnams/ /sems can gyis ni nyes pas bsgribs/ /ji ltar 'dud pa'i dbang gis na/ /gos la tshon bkra mi bkra ba/ /de bzhin 'phen pa'i dbang gis na/ /grol ba'i ye shes bkra mi bkra/ /dri med dbyings la sangs rgyas kyi/ /
10b5(mdo 'grel): mtshan nyid dang ni gnas pa dang/ /phrin las zab pa 'di bshad pa/ /mkha' la cho na gyi ri mo 'dri/ /de bzhin nyidn i thams cad la/ /khyad par med kyang dag gyur pa/ /de bzhin gshegs nyid de yi phyir/ /'gro kun de yi snying po can/ /nyan thos rnams kyi 'byor pas ni/ /'jig rten pa
10b6(mdo 'grel): yi zil gyis gnon/ /rang sangs rgyas kyi sa pa yis/ /nyan thos kyi yang? zil gyis gnon/ /de yis byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /'byor pa'i char yang mi bod do/ /de yis de bzhin gshegs pa yi/ /'byor pa'i char yang mi phod do/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyi 'byor pa ni/ /gang gi
10b7(mdo 'grel): gang du ji ltar dang/ /ji tsam dus gang 'jug pa ni/ /bsam yas dpag tu med par 'dod/ /dbang po lnga rnams gzhan gyur na/ /don kun 'jug dang thams cad kyi/ /yon tan rgya phrag bcu gnyis 'byung/ /'byor pa dam pa thob par 'gyur/ /yid ni gzhan du gyur pa na/ /'byor dang mthun
11a1(mdo 'grel): spyod mi rtog pa'i/ /ye shes shin tu dri med la/ /'byor pa dam pa thob par 'gyur/ /don bcas 'dzin pa gzhan gyur na/ /ji ltar 'dod bzhin longs spyod dag /bstan phyir zhing ni dag pa la/ /'byor pa dam pa thob par 'gyur/ /rnam rtog gzhan du gyur na ni/ /
11a2(mdo 'grel): dus rnams rtag tu ye shes dang/ /las rnams kun la thogs med la/ /'byor pa dam pa thob par 'gyur/ /rten ni gzhan du gyur pa na/ /sangs rgyas dri med gnas la ni/ /mi gnas mya ngan 'das pa yis/ /'byor pa dam pa thob par 'gyur/ /'khrig pa gzhan du
11a3(mdo 'grel): gyur na ni/ sangs rgyas bde bar gnas pa dang/ /mo mthong nyon mong med pa la/ /'byor pa dam pa thob par 'gyur/ /nam mkha' i 'du shes gzhan gyur na/ /bsaMs pI don ni 'byor pa dang/ 'gro gzugs rnam par 'byed pa la/ /'byor pa daM pa thob par 'gyur/ /de ltar
11a4(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas dri med pa'i/ /gnas ni gzhan 'gyur dpag med pas/ /bsam yas bya ba bsgrub pa yi/ /'byor ba dpag tu med par 'dod/ /'di na 'jig rten phyogs phyogs rgyal ba'i legs bshad pas/ /dge ba 'phel ba'i 'jig rten rnam dag mchog tu 'gro/
11a5(mdo 'grel): dge ba ma bsags dge ba 'phel ba'i mchog tu 'gro/ de ltar ma smin smin pa rtag 'gro'ang ma lus min/ /de ltar 'jig rten phyogs phyoD brtan rnams rtag bar dus kun tu/ /byang chub chen po theb dka' yon tan mchog ldan rmad byung can/ /rtag brtan skyabS
11a6(mdo 'grel): med rnams kyi skyabs gang yin pa thob pa de/ /ya mtshan che la tshul bzang spyad phyir yam tshan che ba 'ang med/ /de ni cig car la lar? sgo mang brgya nas chos kyi 'khor lo dang/ /la lar skye ba mi snang la lar skye ba'i spyod pa sna tshogs dang/ /la lar byang chub thams cad la
11a7(mdo 'grel): lar de ni mya ngan 'da' ston kyang/ /de ni gnas de las kyang rnam par g.yo mi mnga' la thams cad mdzad/ /sangs rgyas rnams ni 'di snyam lus can 'di ni bdag giS smin bya zhes 'am/ /'di ni rab tu smi bya na gzhan yang da ltar smin par byed snyam du/ /'du mdzad mi
11b1(mdo 'grel): mnga' bar yang phyogs phyogs kun tu rtag par sgo gsum nas/ /dge ba'i chos rnams kyis ni skye bo rab tu smin par 'gyur ba nyid /ji ltar nyi ma 'bad med phyogs phyog kun tu 'od zer dag /rab 'byams gsal ba mang pos lo tog rnams smin byed pa ltar
11b2(mdo 'grel): de bzhin chos ldan nyi ma'ang rab zhi byed pa chos kyi 'od/ /rab 'byams dag gis phyogs phyog kun tu sems can rnam smin mdzad/ /ji ltar mar me gcig las mar me'i tshogs rab mang/ /dpag med grangs med 'byung yang de la zad pa med/ /de
11b3(mdo 'grel): bzhin smin pa gcig las smin pa'i tshogs rab mang/ /dpag med grangs med 'byung yang de la zad pa med/ /ji ltar rgya mtsho chen po 'di na chu yi ngoms par mi 'gyur zhing/ /chu chen mang po rab tu 'bab pas 'phel bar yang ni mi 'gyur ba/ /de
11b4(mdo 'grel): bzhin sangs rgyas khams kyang dag pa 'jug pa rtag rgyun mi 'chad pas/ /ngoms par mi 'gyur 'phel bar mi 'gyur de 'dir smad du byung ba'i mchog /chos rnams kun gyi de bzhin nyid/ /sgrib gnyis dag pa'i mtshan nyid de/ /dngos po shes pa de la dmigs/ /
11b5(mdo 'grel): dbang zad mi shes mtshan nyid do/ /de bzhin nyid shes thams cad nas/ /bsgoms pa las ni yang dag 'byung/ /sems can kun la rnam kun tu/ /gnyis bskyed mi zad 'bras bu can/ /sku dang gsung dang thugs sprul pa'i/ /'byor pa'i thabs kyi las can te/ /ting
11b6(mdo 'grel): nge 'dzin dang gzungs sgo dang/ /dpag tu med pa gnyis dang ldan/ /rang bzhin chos rdzogs longs spyod dang/ /sprul pa ngag gi tha dad 'jug /'di ni sangs rgyas rnam dag gi /chos dbying rnaM par dag par bshad/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyi sku dbye ba/ /rang bzhin longs spyod
11b7(mdo 'grel): rdzogs pa dang/ /gzhan ni sprul pa'i sku yin te/ /dang po gnyis po'i rten yin no/ /longs spyod rdzogs pa khams kun tu/ /'khor yongs sdud dang zhing dang mtshan/ /sku dang chos rdzogs longs spyod dan/ /mdzad pa dag gis tha dad do/ /rang bzhin sku ni mnyam
12a1(mdo 'grel): phra zhing de dang 'brel ba dang/ /dgyes dgur longs spyod bstan pa la/ /longs spyod rdzogs 'byor rgyur 'dod do/ /sangs rgyas sprul ba dpag med pa/ /sprul pa'i skur ni 'dod pa ste/ /don gnyis phun sum tshogs ba de/ /rnam pa thams cad gnyis la gnod?
12a2(mdo 'grel): bzo dang skye dang byang chub che/ /mya ngan 'das paS rtag ston pa/ /sangs rgyas sprul pa'i sku 'di ni/ /rnam par grol pa'i thabs chen po/ /sku gsum ngag gis sangs rgyas kyi/ /sku bsdus par ni shes bya ste/ /sku gsum dag gis rang bzhin gyis/ /don 'di rten dang bcas par bstan/ /
12a3(mdo 'grel): de bag rten dang dgongs pa dang/ /phrin las kyis ni mnyam ba nyid/ /rang bzhin dang ni rgyun mi 'chad/ /rgyun gyis de dag rtag ba nyid/ /me long ye shes mi g.yo ste/ /ye shes gsum ni de la rten/ /mnyam pa nyid dang so sor rtog /bya ba sgrub pa kho na'o/ /me long ye shes nga
12a4(mdo 'grel): yi med/ /yongs su ma chad rtag tu ldan/ /shes bya kun lam rmongs la/ /rtag tu de la mngon mchog min/ /ye sheS kun gyi rgyu mtshan phyir/ /ye shes 'byung gnas chen po 'dra/ /longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas nyid/ /ye shes gzugs brnyan 'byung phyir te/ /sgom pa dag
12a5(mdo 'grel): pas sems can la/ /mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes 'dod/ /mi gnas zhi bar zhugs pa ni/ /mnyam nyid ye shes yin par 'dod/ /dus rnams rtag tu byams pa dang/ /thugs rje chen po dag dang ldan/ /sems can rnams la mos pa bzhin/ /sangs rgyas sku ni nges par ston/
12a6(mdo 'grel): so sor rtog pa'i ye shes ni shes bya kun la rtag mi thogs/ /ting nge 'dzin dang gzugs rnams kyi/ /gter dang 'dra ba kho na yin/ /'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnams su ni/ /'byor ba thams cad ston mdzad pa/ /the tshom thams cad gcod pa yi/ /chos chen char ni
12a7(mdo 'grel): rab tu 'bebs/ /bya ba sgrub pa'i ye shes ni/ /khams rnams kun tu sna tshogs shing/ /dpag med bsam yas sprul pa yi/ /sems can kun gyi don sgrub pa'o/ /sangs rgyas sprul pa de dag tu/ /mdzad pa grub pa'i bye brag dang/ /grangs dang zhing gis rnam kun tu/ /bsaM
12b1(mdo 'grel): gyi mi khyab shes par bya/ /'dzin pa'i phyir dang sems mnyam phyir/ /yang dag chos rab ston phyir dang/ /bya ba sgrub pa nyid kyi phyir/ /ye shes bzhi po yang dag 'byung/ /tha dad rigs don med phyir dang/ /rdzogs dang thog ma med ba'i phyir/ /sangs rgyas gcig min dri med gnas/ /
12b2(mdo 'grel): tha dad min phyir mang bo 'ang min/ /med pa gang yin de nyid ni/ /yod pa yin ni dam par 'dod/ /rnam pa kun tu mi dmigs pa/ /dmigs pa yin ni mchog tu 'dod/ /sgom pa rnam par mi lta ba'i/ /sgom pa dam par 'dod pa ste/ /thob par lta ba med rnams kyi/ /thob pa yang ni dam par
12b3(mdo 'grel): 'dod/ /bla ma ring dang mtshan ma dang/ /bdag gi brtson 'grus lhag lta ba'i/ /byang chub sems dpa' nga rgyal can/ /byang chub las ni ring zhes 'dod/ /ji skad bshad pa 'di dag kun/ /rtog pa tsam du lta ba yi/ /byang chub sems dpa' rtog pa med pa rnams/ /byang chub thob ces des par
12b4(mdo 'grel): brjod/ /klung dag sa yi 'og tu ma song ba/ /gnas rnams tha dad chu yang tha dad la/ /chu yang chub zhing bya ba tha dad byed/ /chu gnas srogs chags phra mo'i nyer spyad 'gyur/ /rgya mcher song bar gyur pa thams cad kyang/ /gnas rnams gcig cing chu yang che la gcig /bya ba gcig cing
12b5(mdo 'grel): chu na gnas pa yis/ /srog chags mang po rtag tu nyer spyang che// sangs rgyas nyid du ma zhugS brtan pa rnams/ /rten kyang tha dad blo gros tha dad cing/ /rtogs chud rang gi bya ba tha dad la/ /sems can nyung don rtag tu nyer spyad 'gyur/ /sangs rgyas nyid du zhugs na de dag kun/ /rten kyang gcig
12b6(mdo 'grel): cing rtogs pa tshe la gcig /mdzad pa gcig tu 'dres shing rtag par yang/ /sems can tshogs che'i nye bar spyad pa che/ /de ltar sangs rgyas nyid ni dkar po'i chos/ /dpe med ldan phyir phan bde'i rgyu yi phyir/ /bde dge dam pa mi zad 'byung gnas phyir/ /blo ldan byang chub semS
12b7(mdo 'grel): dge blang ba'i rigs/ /byang chub kyi skabs rdzogs so// //sdom ni dang po sgrub dang skyabs rigs dang/ /de bzhin du ni sems bskyed dang/ /rang gzhan don dang de ba nyid don/ /mthu dang yongs smin byang chub bo/ /skyes dang ma skyes 'dzin dang gzung gyur dang/ /grogS?
13a1(mdo 'grel): blangs bdag nyid dang ni nor pa dang/ /ma nor gzhan dang mngon sum du yin gzhan/ /sgras byung tshol ba dang ni lta ba'o/ /'phrogs dang 'dres dang mi mthun phyogs ma 'dres/ /dman dang rgya chen bsgribs dang ma bsgribs dang/ /brtson dang mi
13a2(mdo 'grel): brtson bsags dang ma bsags pa/ /brtan zhugs ring du song ba'i mos pa 'o/ /yid la mi byed mang ba dang/ /le lo rnal 'byor 'khrugs pa dang/ /grogs ngan dge ba zhan pa dang/ /tshul bzhin ma yin yid la byed/ /bag med pa dang thos pa nyung/ /thos dang bsam pa
13a3(mdo 'grel): nyung dus mchog/ zhi ba tsam gyi nga rgyal dang/ /de bzhin ma 'dris yin par 'dod/ /mi skyo ba dang de bzhin skyo/ /bsgrib ba dang ni mi brtson ba/ /tshogs ma bsags ba mos pa yi/ /bar du bcod par shes par bya/ /bsod nams che dang 'gyod pa med/ /yid bde ba dang bde ba che//
13a4(mdo 'grel): chud mi za dang brtan pa dang/ /de bzhin khyad par 'gro ba dang/ /chos kyi mngon par rtogs ba dang/ /bdag dang gzhan don thob pa'i mchog /mngon shes myung ba de dag ni/ /mos pa mi ni phan yon yin/ /'dod pa can gyi de khyi 'dra/ /ting nge 'dzin gyi ru spal
13a5(mdo 'grel): bzhin/ /rang don byed pa'i de bran 'dra/ /gzhan don byed pa'i rgyal po bzhin/ /ji ltar khyi ni rtag tu ltogs shing sdug bsngal gyis nyen mchog mi shes/ /ji ltar ru sbal de ni chu yi nang na kun nas bskums shing 'dug /ji ltar bran ni rtag tu 'jigs shing skrag
13a6(mdo 'grel): pa'i lus kyi rnam par rgyu/ /ji ltar rgyal po yang ni bka' yis yul la dbang sgyur gnas pa ltar/ /de bzhin g.yem dang gnas dang rang gzhan phan bya don byed pa'i/ /mos pa sna tshogs dag gis rtag tu khyad par shes par bya/ /theg pa chen po de la de
13a7(mdo 'grel): mchog tshul bzhin rig nas ni/ /'di na brtan bas de la de nyid rtag par rab tu tshal/ /gang phyir sems can mir gyur pa/ /tshangs med skad cig re re la/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob de'i phyir/ zhum pa dang du blang mi bya/ /gzhan dag la ni zas byin pa'i/ /
13b1(mdo 'grel): bsod nams 'phel bar ji lta bar/ /bdag nyid za ba'i ma yin pa/ /de bzhin gzhan don rten gyi chos/ /bstan la mdo las gsungs pa yi/ /bsod nams chen 'byung thod ba ltar/ /rang gi don gyi rten gyi chos/ /bstan las thob pa ma yin no/ /de ltar 'phaD
13b2(mdo 'grel): pa chen po'i chos ni yongs gyur la/ /blo dang ldan pas rtag tu mos pa che bskyed nas/ /bsod nams rgya che na rgyun mi 'chang dang de 'phel dang/ /yon tan dpag tu med pas bdag nyid chen por 'gyur/ /mos pa'i skabs rdzogs so// //sde snod
13b3(mdo 'grel): dag ni gsum mam gnyis kyang rung/ /bsdus pa'i phyir te rgyu ni dgus 'dod do/ /de ni bag chags rtogs dang zhi ba dang/ /rab tu rtogs bas rnam par grol bar byed/ /mdo dang chos mngon 'dul pa dag /mdor na don ni rnam bzhir 'dod/ /blo dang ldan pas de 
13b4(mdo 'grel): shes nas/ /rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa thog /gnas rnams dang ni mtshan nyid dang/ /chos don smos phyir mdo yin no/ /mngon du'i phyir dang yang yang dang/ /zil gnon rtogs phyir mngon pa'i chos/ /ltung dang 'byung dang ldang ba dang/ /des par 'byung dang gang
13b5(mdo 'grel): zag dang/ /bcas pa dang ni rab dbye dang/ /rnam par nges phyir 'dul ba nyid/ /dmigs pa chos dang nang dang ni/ /phyi dang gnyis ni yin par 'dod/ /don gnyis kyis ni gnyis po rnyed/ /gnyis po dag ni mi dmigs pas/ /yid kyi brjod pas bshad
13b6(mdo 'grel): bzhin don/ /rab dang mngon du snang ba ni/ /brjod las yin par rab 'dzin phyir/ /sems ni ming la gnas pa'i phyir/ /thos la sogs pa'i shes gsum gyis/ /chos kyi dmigs pa rnyed par 'gyur/ /dmigs pa rnam pa gsum rnyed pa/ /sngar bshad
13b7(mdo 'grel): de la yang dag brten/ /rigs gsum pa dang bya ba byed/ /mi gnod rten bcas gzhan yin te/ /mos pa 'jog par byed dang gzhan/ /'dun pa drag por byed ba dang/ /dman dang rdzogs rten rnam pa gnyis/ /brjod dang bcas dang brjod med gnyis/ /shes pa dang
14a1(mdo 'grel): ni tshungs ldan pa/ /rnal 'byor rgyu bdag bcas pa dang/ /de ni 'dres la dmigs pa dang/ /ma 'dres pa la dmigs pa de/ /rnam pa lnga dang rnam bdun 'di/ /nyid yi yongs su shes pa lnga/ /rnam pa sgom dang dan pa ni/ /bzhi dang sum
14a2(mdo 'grel): cu rtsa bdun no/ /de ni lam gnyis rang bzhin te/ /phan yon gnyis dang nod pa dang/ /sbyor ba pa dang dbang sgyur dang/ /chung dang rgya che'i bdag nyid de/ /rnal 'byor rnams kyi yid byed de/ /thams cad bdag nyid yin par 'dod/ /rtag tu gnyis bral 'khrul pa'i rten
14a3(mdo 'grel): gang yin dang gang zhig rnam kun tu/ /brjod par nus ma yin zhing spros pa med pa'i bdag nyid de kho na/ /shes bya spang bya rang bzhin dri med 'dod gang rnam par spangs bya ste/ don ni mkha' gser dang chu ltar nyon mongs pa las rnam dag 'dod/ /'gro ba dag na de las gzhan yang
14a4(mdo 'grel): cung zad yod min la/ /'gro ba ma lus ba yang de la kun tu smongs pa'i blo/ /yod pa kun nas spangs te med la mngon zhen gang yin pa/ /'jig rten rmongs ba'i rnam la che? bas chen 'di ko ji lta bu/ /ji ltar sgyu ma de bzhin du/ /yang dag ma yin kun rtog brjod/ /sgyu ma
14a5(mdo 'grel): byas pa ji lta bar/ /de bzhin gnyis su 'khrul pa brjod/ /ji ltar de la de med pa/ /de bzhin du ni don dam 'dod/ /ji ltar de ni dmigs pa ltar/ /de bzhin du ni kun rdzob 'dod/ /de med na ni de yi rgyu/ /bsal bar dmigs pa ji lta bar/ /de bzhin gnas ni
14a6(mdo 'grel): gzhan gyur na/ /yang dag ma yin rtog pa dmigs/ /ji ltar 'jig rten ma 'khrul pa/ /de yi rgyu la 'dod dgur sbyong/ /de bzhin sdom brtson ma 'khrul ba/ /gnas gzhan gyur pa dgyes dgur spyod/ /de lta bu ni de la yod/ /de yi dngos bo yod ma yin/ /de ltas
14a7(mdo 'grel): sgyu ma la sogs pa/ /yod dang med pa nyid du brjod/ /de la yod pa med ma yin/ /med pa yod pa nyi ma yin/ /sgyur ma dag la sogs pa la/ /yod med khyad bar med pa'ang brjod/ /de bzhin gnyis snang de la yod/ /de yi dngos po yod ma yin/ /
14b1(mdo 'grel): de ltar gzugs la sogs pa la/ /yod dang med pa nyid du brjod/ /de la yod ba med ma yin/ /med ba yod ba nyid ma yin/ /gzugs la sogs pa dag la ni/ /yod med khyad par med pa'ang brjod/ /sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa yi/ /mdza' rnamS
14b2(mdo 'grel): dgag par bya phyir dang/ theg pa dman bas 'gro ba dag /dgag par bya phyir 'dod pa yin/ /'khrul pa'i rgyu dang 'khrul ba ni/ /gzugs can min rnam rig bar 'dod/ /med phyir cig shos kyang med 'gyur/ /sgyu ma'i glang po'i gzugs
14b3(mdo 'grel): 'dzin pa/ /'khrul phyir gnyis su brjod ba ste/ /de la ji bzhin gnyis med kyang/ /gnyis po dag tu nye bar dmigs/ /keng rus kyis ni gzugs 'dzin pa/ /'khrul phyir gnyis su brjod pa ste/ /de la ji bzhin gnyis med
14b4(mdo 'grel): kyang/ /gnyis po dag tu nya bar dmigs/ /'khrul pa'i mtshan nyid chos gang yin/ /de bzhin yod dang de bzhin med/ /yod med khyad par med pa'i phyir/ /yid dang med pa sgyu ma 'dra/ /gnyen po'i chos ni gang yin pa/ /de bzhin med dang de
14b5(mdo 'grel): bzhin yod/ /de bzhin med? phyir mtshan nyid med/ /sgyu ma dang yang 'dra bar bstan/ /sgyu ma'i rgyal po sgyu ma yi/ /rgyal po gzhan gyis pham pa ltar/ /gang dag gis ni chos mthong ba'i/ /rgyal sras de dag nga rgyal med/ /sangs rgyas
14b6(mdo 'grel): rnam sangs rgyas mchog rnams kyis de dang de las 'dus byas dag /gsungs pa sgyu ma rmi lam smig rgyu gzugs brnyan de dang 'dra mig yong dang/ /brag tsa? lte? bu dang ni chu zla'i gzugs 'dra sprul dang 'drar shes bya/ /drug dang drug dang gnyiS
14b7(mdo 'grel): dang drug tshan gnyis dang gsum po re rer 'dod/ /yang dag min rtog yang dag min/ /yang dag ma yin min mi rtog /rtog min mi rtog ma yin ba/ /shes bya thams cad yin bar brjod/ /rang gi khams las gnyis bo zhing/ ma rig nyon
15a1(mdo 'grel): mongs lhan cig tu/ 'jug pa'i rnam rtog rab 'byung ste/ rdzas gnyis rnam par spangs pa yin/ /dmigs pa'i khyad par thob pa yi/ /rang gi dbyings la gnas ldan phyir/ /de nyid gnyis su snang med pa/ /'jug ste lngags dang mda'
15a2(mdo 'grel): bzhin no/ /sems ni gnyis su snang ba ste/ de bzhin chags sogs snang ba 'am/ dad la sogs pa snang bar 'dod/ /nyon mongs dge chos yod ma yin/ /sems ni sna tshogs snang ba dang/ /rnam ba sna tshogs can du 'jug /de la snang de yod
15a3(mdo 'grel): dang med/ /de phyir chos kyi ma yin no/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis sems can la/ phan gdags phyir ni mtshan bzhi dang/ /mtshan nyid dang ni mchon pa dag /rab tu dbye bas yang dag bshad/ /sems ni ltar bcas gang yin dang/ /
15a4(mdo 'grel): de yi gnas skabs mi 'gyur ba/ /'di ni 'dor na mtshan gzhi ste/ /rab tu dbye na tshad med do/ /ji ltar brjod don 'du shes kyi/ /rgyu mtshan de yi bag chags dang/ /de las kyang don snang ba ni/ /kun brtags pa yi mtshan nyid 'dod/ /
15a5(mdo 'grel): ming dang don ni ji lta bar/ /don dang ming? bu snang ba gang/ /yang dag min rtog rgyu mtshan ni/ /kun tu brtags pa'i mtshan nyid do/ /rnam gsum rnam gsum snang ba can/ /bzung dang 'dzin pa'i mtshan nyid de/ /yang dag ma yin kun rtogs
15a6(mdo 'grel): ni/ gzhan gyi dbang gi mtshan nyid do/ /med dang yod nyid gang yin dang/ /yod dang med pa mnyam nyid dang/ /ma zhi ni? dang rnam mi rtog /yongs su grub pa'i mtshan nyid do/ /rgyu 'thun chos la dmigs nas ni/ /tshul bzhin yid la
15a7(mdo 'grel): byed pa dang/ /sems kyi dbyings ba la gnas pa dang/ /don yod pa dang med par mthong/ /de nas mnyam pa nyid du 'gyur/ /'phags rigs shin tu dri med pa/ /mnyam dang khyad 'phags 'bri med cing/ /'phel ba mtshan nyid med par
15b1(mdo 'grel): 'dod/ /sa bon gzhan du gyur ba'i phyir/ /gnas don lus su snang ba dag /gzhan du gyur pa zag med dbyings/ /de ni rten kun 'gro ba can/ /yid dang 'dzin dang rnam par rtog /gyur phyir rnam par mi rtogs pa/ /zhi dang ye shes laS

15b6(mdo 'grel): pa yis/ /skye med 'gag med gzod nas zhi/ /rang bzhin mya ngan 'das pa gru ba/ /thog ma dang ni de nyid gzhan nyid dang/ /rang gi mtshan nyid rang dang gzhan du gyur/ /kun nas nyon mongs pa dang khyad par la/ /skye ba med pa'i chos

16a2(mdo 'grel): bral min 'di dman pa'o/ /de gnyis 'phags pa'i lam thob pa/ /srid pa dag tu sgyur ba'i phyir/ /bsam gyis mi khyab sgyur ba yin/ skye ba dang i yang dag ldan/ /gcig ni smon lam dbang gis na/ /skye bar rab tu sgrub par byed/ /cig shos

16a6(mdo 'grel): pa'o/ /mthu ni rnam pa bzhi dag gis/ /dga' dang nges par mi skyo dang/ /mi mthun phyogs dang gnyen po la/ /sgrub pa rnam pa bzhi yin no/ /rab dang yang dag nod pa dang/ /gzhan la sbyin par 'dun pa dang/ /go cha dang ni smon lam dang//
16a7(mdo 'grel): mngon par dga' dang bya ba'i yid/ /sbyin sogs rnam pa drug la ni/ /mthu thob pa dang yongs smin dang/ /mchod pa dang ni rten pa la/ /yang dag spro ba mchog dang brtse/ /ma byas ngan par byas pa la/ /ngo tsha 'gyod dang yul la dbang?
16b1(mdo 'grel): skyo la dgra po'i 'dus shes dang/ /'god dang brjod pa'i blo gros so/ /sbyin sogs rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi/ /rten yin dbang phyug la sogs min/ /gnyis po dag la skyon dang ni/ /yon tan so so yang dag rigs/ /bsags pa rjes su dran
