16b4(mdo 'grel): ba'i sems can la/ /mi dga' ba dang dga' ba'o/ /sgom pa bcos dang yang dag la/ /ma dad pa dang dad pa dang/ /dang du mi len yid byed dang/ /lung bstan nges par dga' ba'o/ /phyi ma'i tshe la mthong ba'i phyir/ /'jug sems mnyam par lta
16b5(mdo 'grel): ba'i phyir/ /mchog chos rnams la zhugs pa yis/ /bdag nyid mchog tunges 'dzin phyir/ /pha rol phyin bcu'i rgyus byung ba/ /dge ba yid la byed 'di dag /rtag tu byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /khams ni rtsh par byed pa yin/ /rgyas dang lhag pa'i
16b6(mdo 'grel): bsam dang chen po ni/ /brtan pa'i yongs su tshol ba yin par 'dod/ /de dag giS ni spang dang bcas pa dang/ /spang ba med dang de bzhin dbang 'byor pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshol ba ani/ /sku med pa dang bcas dang sku thob dang/ /sku yongs rdzoD
16b7(mdo 'grel): dang/ nga rgyal mang ba dang/ /nga rgyal phra ba dang nga rgyal med bar 'dod/ /bstan bcos gzugs dang gzugs min la/ /mtshan dangde bzhin nad med dang/ /mngon shes rnams kyi dbang phyug dang/ /de zad mi shes nyid kyi rgyu/ /rgyal ba'i sras rnams kyis ni
17a1(mdo 'grel): med dang yod pa dang/ /sgro 'dog skur pI rtog dang gcig nyid du ma nyid/ /rang dang khyad par rtog dang ming don ji bzhin du/ /mngon par zhen pa'i rtog pa yang dag spang bar bya/ /de ltar blo gros dge ba brtson 'grus drag brten nas/ /de bzhin
17a2(mdo 'grel): nyid bcas gnyis kyi chos nyid yongs bcal? ba/ /de phyir rtag tu skye gu rnams kyi ston par 'gyur/ /de ni rgya mtsho bzhin du yon tan rnams kyi gang/ /chos yongs su tshol ba'i skabs rdzogs so// //brtan pa rtsams ni srogs dang longs spyod tshigs
17a3(mdo 'grel): ches rnyed cing snying po med pa dang/ /rab dga' i yid kyis sems can sdug bsngal rnams la sbyin rnams rgya chen rtag gtong na/ /chos spangs skye gu rnams la rnam pa kun tu phan byed tshags chen rnyed min zhing/ /shin tu btang yang zad med 'phel 'gyur ba lta
17a4(mdo 'grel): lan cig ma yin smos ci dgos/ /gang phyir rang rigs chos bas bcom ldan 'das kyis ma bstan khu chu ltar/ /thugs rje'i bdag nyid sprul chen lta bu dag gis rigs bshad chos rnams kyis/ /skye bo nyid kyis chos la kun nas drangs te /nyid zhi shal?
17a5(mdo 'grel): gyi sgo/ /rnam par dag pa rgya che thun mong zad mi shes la yang dag bkod/ /de lta rnal 'byor can gyis sgom pa gang yin te ni don med min/ /de lta bde bar gshegs kyi bstan pa gang yin de yang don med yin/ /gal te thos pa tsam gyis don mthong gyur
17a6(mdo 'grel): na sgom pa don med 'gyur/ /gal te ma thos par yang sgom 'jug 'gyur/ stan pa don med 'gyur/ /sems dpa' mchog gi ston pa ni/ /lung dang rtogs dang dbang 'byor dang/ /de dang gzugs ni thams cad dang/ /nam mkha' las kyang 'byung ba yin/ /rgya che
17a7(mdo 'grel): the chom spong ba dang/ gzung 'os de nyid gnyis ston ga 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /ston pa phun tshogs yin shes bya/ /sems dpa' mchog gi stan pa ni/ /'jam zhing rgyags gral mi skyo dang/ /gsal zhing sna tshogs rigs ba dang/ /go zhing zang zing med kun 'gro
17b1(mdo 'grel): rgyal sras tshig ni mi zhan pa/ /snyan zhing legs bshad grags pa dang/ /ci rigs pa dang zang zing med/ ran zhing de bzhin yangs pa yin/ /bstan dang de bzhin bshad pa dang/ /theg dang mthun dang bde ba dang/ /grags pa dang ni ci rigs dang/ /nges par 'byung dang mthun
17b2(mdo 'grel): pa'i phyir/ /de mdor sems dpa' mchog rnams kyi/ /yi ge phun tshogs yin shes bya/ /bde gshegs gsung ni 'tha' yas te/ /yan lag drug cu bsam mi khyab/ /dag tshig shin tu rigs pa dang/ /bstan dang rnam 'byed the tshom bcod/ /lan mang byed dang
17b3(mdo 'grel): ldan pa ni/ /mgo smos rnam spros so/ rnam pa/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyi ston pa ni/ /'khor gsum gyis ni dag pa ste/ /'di ni nyes pa brgyad dag dang/ /bul pa nyid du shes par bya /le lo dang ni mi go dang /skabs mi 'byed dang ma nges dang/ /the tshom dag
17b4(mdo 'grel): ni mi gcod dang/ /de dang bral ba brtan mi byed/ /skyo ba dang ni ser sna nyid/ /'di dag gtam gyi nyes par 'dod/ /de dag med phyir sangs rgyas kyi bshad pa bla na med par 'gyur/ /dad dang dga' dang blo rnams kyi/ /rgya phyir chos 'di dge ba yin/ /don rnams gnyis ldan
17b5(mdo 'grel): gzung smra dang/ /yon tan bzhi can tshangs spyod ston/ /gzhan dang thun mong ma yin ldan pa dang/ /khams gsum nyon mongs rnam spong rdzogs byed dang/ /ngo bo nyid dag dri ma dag pa ste/ /tshangs spyod yon tan ba ni ldan yin par 'dod/ /gzhug pa ldem por dgongs pa dang
17b6(mdo 'grel): mtshan nyid ldem por dgongs pa dang/ gnyen po ldem bor dgongs pa dang/ /bsgyur ba ldem por dgongs pa ste/ /nyan thos dang ni ngo bo nyid/ /de bzhin nyes pa 'dus pa dang/ /brjod pa zab pa nyid la ni/ /ldem por dgongs pa 'di rnam bzhi/ /mnyam nyid dang ni don
17b7(mdo 'grel): gzhan dang/ /de bzhin dus gzhan dang/ /gang zag gis ni bsam pa la/ /dgongs pa rnam pa bzhir shes bya/ /sangs rgyas chos la snyas pa dang/ /le lo bcung zad chog 'dzin dang/ /nga rgyal 'dod chags spyod pa dang/ /'gyod dang ma nges ldan pa ni//
18a1(mdo 'grel): sems can rnams kyi sgrib pa ste/ /de yi gnyen por theg mchog gsungs/ /nges de'i bar du bcod pa yi/ /nyes pa thams cad spong bar 'gyur/ /gang zhig tshig gam don sgo nas/ /tshig bcad gnyis 'dzin rab sbyor ba/ /sems
18a2(mdo 'grel): can blo ldan mchog de yis/ /yon tan rnam bcu thob 'gyur te/ /khams ni zad par rtas pa dang/ /'chi ba'i tshe na rab dga' mchog /ji ltar 'dod par skye ba dang/ /kun tu tshe rabs dran pa dang/ /sangs rgyas rnams dang phrad pa dang/ /de las theg mchog
18a3(mdo 'grel): thos pa dang/ /mos pa blo dang bcas pa dang/ /sgo gnyis byang chub myur thob pa'o/ /de ltar blo bzang skyo ba med ldan brtse ba can/ /snyan par rab grags cho ga bzang zhes ldan ba yi/ /byang chub sems dpa' lags par smra ba yin pa ste/ /bshad pas skye po'i
18a4(mdo 'grel): na ngan nyi ma bzhin du lha ma/ /bshad pa'i skabs rdzogs so// //blo ldan gnyis la log nyid dang/ /yang dag nyid rnam spangs gsum gyis/ /gang zag dang ni chos dag la/ /bdag med rnam gnyis kun shes nas/ /don shes pas ni chos rnams kun
18a5(mdo 'grel): gzings dang 'dra ba nyid du rig /thos pas chog par 'dzin spong la/ /nges na chos shes zhes pa brjod/ /so so'i skye bo'i shes pa yis/ /de bzhin du ni gnyis rtogs nas/ /shes ba de yongs rdzogs bya'i phyir/ /mthun pa'i chos ni rab tu sgrub/ /de nas de ni sa
18a6(mdo 'grel): dang por/ /byang chub sems dpa' de bdag nyid/ /kun nas mnyam par 'jig rten las/ /'das pa'i ye shes bla med thog/ /mthong bas spang bya'i nyon mongs rnams/ /thams cad yang dag zad byas nas/ /shes bya'i sgrib pa spang bya'i phyir/ /sgom pa la ni rab tu sbyor//
18a7(mdo 'grel): rnam 'jog rnam par mi rtogs pa'i/ /ye shes lhan cig spyod pa yi/ /de bzhin sa ni lhag ma la/ /mthun pa yi ni chos spyod do/ /blo ldan gang du sgrub pa'i yul/ /legs par rnyed dang gnas bzang dang/ sa bzang ba dang grogs bzang dang/ /rnal 'byor bde ba'i yon tan
18b1(mdo 'grel): ldan/ /byang chub sems dpa' thos mang dang/ /bden mthong smra mkhas brtse bcan/ /skyo med skyes bu dam pa ni/ /chen po yin par shes par bya/ /dmigs pa bzang dang ston pa bzang?/ /thabs bzang ? dang nges 'byung dang/ /sbyor ba bzang po'i bdag nyid dang/ /yang dag smon lam yin
18b2(mdo 'grel): par bshad do/ /dga' dang dal bar skye pa dang/ /nad med pa dang ting nge 'dzin/ /rnam par 'byed pa'i byed rgyu ni/ /sngon chad bsod nams byas pa nyid/ /chos kyi dbyings ni ma gtogs par/ /gang phyir chos med de yi phyir/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis de dag las/ /nges 'byung
18b3(mdo 'grel): chags sogs yin par dgongs/ /chos kyi dbyings ni ma gtogs par/ /gang phyir chos med yi phyir/ /kun nas nyon mongs bstan pa la/ /blo ldan dgongs pa de yin 'dod/ /gang phyir chags sogs de nyid la/ /tshul bzhin 'jug pa de yi phyir/ /de las rnam grol 'gyur des na//
18b4(mdo 'grel): de yi de dag las nges 'byung/ /sems can ched du dmyal ba'i srid pas gnas pa yi/ /sdug bsngal mi bzang cis kyang rgyal sras la gnod min/ /ji srid yon tan skyon gyis theg pa dman zhugs pa'i/ /rnam tog dge ba sna tshogs blo ldan gnod byed yin/ /blo dang ldan pa
18b5(mdo 'grel): dmyal bar gnas pa dus zhun tu/ /byang chub dri med yangs pa'i bar du gcod byed min/ /theg pa gzhan la rab bsil rnam gtog bdag phan pa/ /rab tu bde bar gnas kyang bar du bcod par byed/ /chos med pa dang dmigs pa dang/ /kun nas nyon mongs med rnam dag /sgyu ma la
18b6(mdo 'grel): sogs 'dra ba dang/ /de bzhin nam mkha' 'drar shes bya/ /ji ltar tshul bzhin bris pa'i ri mo la/ /mthon dman med kyang snang ba de bzhin du/ /yang dag ma yin rtog la rnam kun tu/ /gnyis po rtag tu med kyang snang bar 'gyur/ /ji ltar chu rnyogs pa las dang ba na/ /dang ba nyid de de las
18b7(mdo 'grel): rgyal? min las/ /de ni de la dri ma bral bar zad/ /de bzhin rang sems dag la tshul de nyid/ /sems ni rtag tu rang bzhin 'od gsal 'dod/ /de ni blo bur nyes pas ma rungs byas/ /chos nyid sems las gzhan pa sems gzhan ni/ /'od gsal ma yin rang bzhin la brjod do/ /byang chub sems
19a1(mdo 'grel): dpa' sems can la/ /bu gcig pa la bya ba bzhin/ /rkang gi khong nas byams pa che/ /de ltas rtag phan byed par 'dod/ /sems can rnams la phan byed phyir/ /de las chags skyes ltung mi 'gyur/ /'di yi zhe sdang rnam kun tu/ /sems can kun dang 'gal bar 'gyur/ /ji
19a2(mdo 'grel): ltar phug ron rang gi bu rtsa mchog byams/ /rang gi bu de nye bar 'khyud nas 'dug /de 'dra ba la khong khro 'gal ba ltar/ /brtser bcas lus can bu la'ang de dang 'dra/ /gang phyir byams pa de phyir khong khro 'gal/ /gang phyir zhi ba de phyir gnod sems 'gal/ /gang phyir don
19a3(mdo 'grel): byed de phyir sgyu sems 'gal/ /gang phyir sim byed de phyir 'jigs byed 'gal/ /sman bzang po la nad pa bzhin/ /'khor ba la ni 'jug par byed/ /nad pa la ni sman pa bzhin/ /sems can rnams la sgrub par byed/ /bran ma grub pa ji bzhin du/ /bdag nyid la ni sgrub
19a4(mdo 'grel): par byed/ /zong la tshong pa ji bzhin du/ /'dod pa dag la sgrub par byed/ /gos la brtso brlag mkhan bzhin du/ /las la rab tu sgrub bar byed/ /bu gzhon pa la pha bzhin du/ /sems can mi 'tshe sgrub par byed/ /me don gnyer ba btsub shing ltar/ /rtag par
19a5(mdo 'grel): rab tu sgrub par byed/ /yid brtan bzhin du lhag pa'i sems/ /ma rdzogs pa la sgrub par byed/ /sgyu ma mkhan ltar shes bya la/ /shes rab kyis ni sgrub par byed/ /de ni byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /ji ltar gang du sgrub par 'dod/ /de ltar rtag tu brtson 'grus rgya chen ldan
19a6(mdo 'grel): gnyis yongs smin par bya la rab brtson de/ /rim gyis dri med mi rtog blo mchog gis/ grub pa bla na med par rab tu 'gro/ sgrub pa'i skabs rdzogs so// //skal pa grangs med nges 'byung zhing/ /mos pa rnam par 'phel byed pa/ /ji ltar chu yis
19a7(mdo 'grel): rgya mtsho bzhin/ /dge chos rnams kyis yang dag rdzogs/ /de bzhin du ni tshogs bsags pa'i/ /rgyal sras bzod nas dag pa po/ /legs par shes shing sems dge ba/ /sgom pa la ni rab tu sbyor/ /de tshe chos kyi rgyun la ni/ /sangs rgyas rnams las zhi
19b1(mdo 'grel): gnas dang/ /ye shes yangs pa thob bya'i phyir/ /gdams ngag rgya chen snyed par 'gyur/ /de nas dang por sdom brtson de/ /mdo yi sde la sogs pa'i chos/ /mi gnyis don ni rnam 'byed pa/ /mdo sogs ming la sems 'jog go/ de nas de ni rim bzhin du/ /tshig rab dbye la
19b2(mdo 'grel): spyod byed cing/ /so so'i nang la tshul bzhin du/ /de yi don yang rnam par dpyod/ /de na de dag ni nges bzung nas/ /chos la kun sdom par byed/ /de yi don ni thob bya'i phyir/ /de nas de ni smon par byed/ /yid kyi brjod pas rgyun chags su/ /gtsal bya so sor brtag par bya/ /yid
19b3(mdo 'grel): la byed pa brjod med pa/ /ro cig pas kyang dpyad par bya/ /chos kyi ming ni bsdoms pa'ang 'di/ /zhi gnas lam du shes par bya/ /lhag mthong lam ni de don rnams/ /rnam par dpyod par shes par bya/ /zung du 'brel pa'i lam ni de/ /bsdoms pa yin par shes par bya/ /zhum pa'i
19b4(mdo 'grel): sems ni rab bzung ste/ /rgod pa yang ni zhi bar bya/ /de nas dmigs pa de la ni/ /mnyam par gyur na btang snyoms bzhag/ de la rtag tu bya ba dang/ /gus par byas te sbyar bar bya/ /dmigs pa la ni sems gtad nas/ /de rgyun rnam par g.yeng mi bya/ /rnam g.yeng myur du
19b5(mdo 'grel): brtogs byas nas/ /de la slar ni blan par bya/ /blo ldan gong nas gong du yang/ /sems ni nang du sdu bar bya/ /de nas yon tan mthong ba'i phyir/ /ting nge 'dzin la sems 'dul lo/ /rnam g.yeng nyes pa mthong ba'i phyir/ /de la mi dga' zhi bar bya/ /rnab sems yid mi bde la sogs//
19b6(mdo 'grel): langs pa de bzhin zhi bar bya/ /de nas bsdoms brtson can gyis ni/ /sems la mngon par 'du byed bcas/ /rang gis ngang gis 'byung ba 'thob/ /de goms pa las 'du mi byed/ /de nas de yis lus dang sems/ /shin tu sbyangs pa che thob nas/ /yid la byed dang bcas shes bya//
19b7(mdo 'grel): de yis de ni 'phel byas nas/ /'phel ba ring du 'gro ba yis/ /dngos gzhi'i gnas pa des thob po/ /mngon shes don du gnyer bas de/ /sbyangs na las su rung ba'i mchog/ bsam gtan las thob mngon par shes/ /mngon par sgrub pa'i sgo nas de/ /sangs rgyas dpag tu med
20a1(mdo 'grel): pa la/ /mchad pa'i phyir dang mnyam na pa'i phyir/ /'jig rten khams ni rnams su 'gro/ /'dis ni sangs rgyas dpag med la/ /bskal dpag med pa bsnyen bkur byas/ /de la bsnyen bkur byas pa'i phyir/ /sems ni las rung mchog tu 'gyur/ /de nas de dag sngon rol du//
20a2(mdo 'grel): phan yon? lnga ni 'thob 'gyur te/ /des na rnam par dag pa'i snod/ /bla na med pa nyid 'gyur 'di/ /lus la gnas ngan len pa kun/ /skad cig re re la zad 'gyur/ /lus dang sems ni kun du yang/ /shin tu sbyangs pas gangbar 'gyur/ /chos rnams snang ba thams cad du/ /yongs
20a3(mdo 'grel): su chad pa med rtags 'gyur/ /yang dag pa yi rgyu mtshan ni/ /ma brtags pa dag rab tu mthong/ /de bzhin chos skur brjod dang/ /rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir/ /blo dang ldan pas rnam kun tu/ /rtag tu rgyu yongs 'dzin par byed/ /de nas de 'drar gyur pa yi/ /byang chub sems dpa' 
20a4(mdo 'grel): mnyam bzhag pas/ /yid kyi brjod pa ma gtogs bar/ /don kun rab tu mi mthong po/ /chos kyi snang ba 'phel bya'i phyir/ brtson 'grus btan pa kun tu brtsom/ chos kyi snang ba 'phel nas ni/ /sems tsam la ni gnas par 'gyur/ /de nas don kun snang ba ni/ /sems su rab
20a5(mdo 'grel): tu mthong bar 'gyur/ /de tshe de yi bzung ba yi/ /rnam par g.yeng ba de spongs 'gyur/ /de nas de la 'dzin pa yi/ /rnam par g.yeng ba 'ba' zhig lus/ de tshe bar chad med pa yi/ /ting nge 'dzin la myur du reg/ 'di ltar de yi 'jug thogs su/ /'dzin pa'i rnaM pa g.yeng ba spong//
20a6(mdo 'grel): 'di dag go rim bzhin du ni/ /gro bar gyur sogs yin zhes bya/ /de nas de ni 'jig rten las/ /'das pa'i ye shes bla med pa/ /rnam par mi rtog dri ma med/ /'dzin pa gnyis dang bral ba thob/ /de 'di'i gnas yongs gyur pa ste/ /sa ni dang po yin par 'dod/ /'di de bskal pa dpa' ?
20a7(mdo 'grel): med kyis/ /shin tu rnam par dag bar 'gyur/ /chos kyi dbyings ni mnyam pa nyid/ /rab tu rtogs nas de yi tshe/ /rtag tu sems can thams cad la/ /bdag dang mtshungs pa'i sems thob ste/ /sems can rnams la bdag med dang/ /sdug bsngal dang ni don bya dang/ /lan mi re la
20b1(mdo 'grel): 'di sems snyoms/ /rgyal sras gzhan dang 'dra ba yin/ /des ni khams gsum 'dus byas rnams/ /yang dag ma yin kun rtogs par/ /ye shes shin tu rnam dang bas gnyis su med pa'i don gyis mthong/ /de dag med pa'i ngo bo ni/ /mthong bas spang bya rnams las grol/ /des na de tshe ma thong ba'i
20b2(mdo 'grel): lam/ /thob pa zhes ni nges par brjod/ /sa med pa'i stong pa nyid shes shed/ /de bzhin yod pa'i stong nyid dang/ /rang bzhin yod pa'i stong nyid dang/ /rang bzhin yod pa nyid shes bya/ /stong pa shes pa zhes brjod do/ /mtshan med bzhi ni rnam rtog rnams/ /yang dag zad pa yin zhes bya/ /smon
20b3(mdo 'grel): pa med par gyur pa de/ /yang dag ma yin kun rtog go/ rgyal sras byang chub phyogs mthun pa/ /rnam pa sna tshogs thams cad ni/ /rtag tu mthong ba'i lam de dang/ /lhan cig tu ni thob bar 'dod/ /gang zhig blo yis 'gro ba 'dus byas tsam/ /bdag med sdug bsngal rgyas ba tsam
20b4(mdo 'grel): shes te/ /don med rang bzhin bdag lta rnam spangs nas/ /bdag nyid che lta don chen brten pa gang/ /'di ni bdag lta med par bdag tu lta/ /sdug bsngal med par shin tu sdug bsngal 'gyur/ /rang la phan byas bdag la ji lta bar/ /don kun byed la lan kyang re ba med/ /gang zhig grol
20b5(mdo 'grel): ba mchog gis sems grol la/ /'ching ba mi bzad yun yang ring por bcings /sdug bsngal mthar thug pa ni ma mthong yang/ /rab tu sbyor ba nyid byed byed ba nyid/ /'di ni 'jig rten tshe gcig rang sdug bskur mi nus/ /'jig rten gnas pa srid du gzhan sdug bsngal/ /bsdom
20b6(mdo 'grel): pa smos ci dgos te bsam du med/ /byang chub sems dpa' de las bzlog pa yin/ /rgyal sras sems can rnams la dga' ba dang/ /byams pa gang yin sbyor dang mi skyo gang/ /de ni srid bdag na ngo mtshar che/ /sems can bdag dang mtshungs phyir de lta 'ang min/ /de nas 'di ni lhag
20b7(mdo 'grel): ma yi/ /sa rnams bsgom pa'i lam 'di la/ /ye shes rnam pa gnyis po dag sgom phyir rab tu sbyar bar byed/ /rnam par mi rtog ye shes de/ /sangs rgyas chos ni spyod bar byed/ /gzhan ni ji bzhin rnam 'jig pa/ /sems can rnams ni yongs smin byed/ /grangs med gnyis ni rdzogs 
21a1(mdo 'grel): pa yis/ /sgom pa yi ni mthar phyin te/ /sgom pa tha ma thob nas ni/ /byang chub sems dpa' dbang bskur ba/ /rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin/ /rtog pas mi shigs thob nas ni/ /gnas gzhan gyur pa mthar thug pa/ /sgrib ba kun gyi dri med dang/ /gang la gnas na
21a2(mdo 'grel): sems can kun/ /phan phyir rab tu sgrub byed pa/ /rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa yis/ /go 'phang bla na med pa 'thob/ /de ltar mthod dka' i thub pa rtag mthong ba/ /thos pa mnyam med las byung rab dang ba'i/ /shugs kyi rtag par shin tu sems chim la/ /ji lta bur na don
21a3(mdo 'grel): chen 'gyur ma yin/ /chos kyi sgo la rnam par gnas pa la/ /de bzhin gshegs rtag mngon sum 'doms mdzad cing/ /co nas 'dren zhing nyes pa'i tshad ching nas/ /tshan gyi drangs te byang chub la mgod do/ /sangs rgyas rnams ni rtag tu rang don yang dag sbyor la legs
21a4(mdo 'grel): par bsngags pa dang/ /log par sbyar la smod mjad gnas dang rnam 'byed lhur len mchog gi sems can la/ /gang zhig spangs dang bsten pas bde gshegs bstan pa 'di' rnal 'byor yangs 'gyur ba/ /bar chad mthun pa'i chos ni rnam pa thams cad
21a5(mdo 'grel): rgyal rnams tshul bzhin 'di na ston/ /de ni mthong ba rab dag mi rtog ye shes kyi/ /'jig rten thams cad zil mnan mun pa chen po yang/ /rnam pa kun tu bsal nas nyi ma chen po dag/ shar ba bzhin du 'gro ba rnams la lha me'o/ /de ltar rtag tu dge ba bsags
21a6(mdo 'grel): pas rab gang zhing/ /thub pa las ni rtag tu gdams ngag che thob pa'i/ /sems dpa' mchog ni sems kyi ting 'dzin rab yangs pa/ /thob nas yon tan rgya mtsho'i pha rol 'gro bar 'gyur/ /gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pa'i skabs rdzogs so// //sdom ni
21a7(mdo 'grel): mos pa mang ba nyid dang ni/ /chos tshol ba dang bshad pa dang/ /de bzhin sgrub dang yang dag pa'i/ /gdams dag rjes su bstan pa yin/ /ji ltar nags tshal dang ni lus can ri po dang/ /chu bo rnams kyi rten ni kun nas sa yin pa/ /de bzhin mkhas pa rnams kyi las rnams gsum
21b1(mdo 'grel): po yang/ /kun nas sbyin pa la sogs dge ba yin par brjod/ /shin tu dka' ba'i las ni ngo bo sna tshogs pa/ /bskal pa mang pos tshar phyin mngon brtson bdag nyid can/ /rgyal sras rnams kyi? lus dang ngag sems rang bzhin gyi/ /las rnams dag gis 'di na yid 'byung 'gyur
21b2(mdo 'grel): ba med/ /ji ltar bdag la phan 'dod dug dang mtshon dang ni/ /gnam lcags lce dang dgra las rang gi lus bzlog pa/ /de bzhin rgyal sras theg pa dman pa rnam gnyis las/ /las rnams gsum gyi bdag nyidzlog par byed pa yin/ /rtag tu rnam par mi rtog las
21b3(mdo 'grel): can las min zhing/ /las kyi bya ba dang rnam gsum la mi lta ste/ /des na 'dis ni de thabs yang dag gzung ba'i phyir/ /las rnams dag pa mdza' yas de yis pha rol 'gro/ thabs dang ldan pa'i las kyi skabs rdzogs so// //grangs dang de yi mtshan nyid
21b4(mdo 'grel): go rims dang/ /nges pa'i tshig dang goms dang yon tan dang/ /de dag rab dbye sdu dang mi mthun phyogs/ /yon tan phan tshun rnam nges yin zhes bya/ /longs spyod dang lus phun sum tshogs pa dang/ /'khor rtsom phun sum tshogs pa mngon mtho dang/ /rtag tu nyon
21b5(mdo 'grel): mongs dbang nyid mi 'gro dang/ /bya ba rnams la phyin ci ma log pa'o/ /sems can don la rab brtson pa/ /gtong dang mi gnod bzod pas byed/ /gnas dang grol ba bzhir bcas pas/ /rang don rnam pa thams cad spyod/ /mi 'phongs pa dang rnam par mi 'tshe dang/ /rnam 'tshe bzod dang bya bas
21b6(mdo 'grel): mi skyo dang/ dga' byed legs par brjod par de yi phyir/ /gzhan gyi don ni rang gi don yin no/ /longs spyod mngon par mi dga' dang/ /rab gus gnyis la mi skyo dang/ /rnal 'byor rnam par mi rtog pa/ /theg chen mdza' dag 'dir zad do/ /yul rnams la ni ma chags lam//
21b7(mdo 'grel): de thob rnam g.yeng sdoms pa'i gzhan/ /sems can mi gtong 'phel ba dang/ /sgrib pa rnam par sbyod ba'i gzhan/ /bslab gsum dbang du mdzad nas ni/ /rgyal bas pha rol phyin pa drug yang dag bshad de dang po gsum/ /tha ma gnyis kyis rnam pa gnyis/ gcig ni
22a1(mdo 'grel): gsum char la/ /yang gtogs/ /sbyin pa mi mthun phyogs nyams dang/ /rnam par mi rtogs ye shes ldan/ /'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/ /sems can rnam smon byed rnam gsum/ /tshul khrims mi mthun phyogs nyams dang/ rnam par mi rtog ye shes
22a2(mdo 'grel): ldan/ /'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/ /sems can rnam smin byed rnam gsum/ /bzod pa mi mthun phyogs nyams dang/ /rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/ /'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/ /sems can rnam smin byed rnam gsum/ /brtson 'grus mi mthun phyogs
22a3(mdo 'grel): nyams dang/ /rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/ /'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/ /sems can rnam smin byed rnam gsum/ /bsam gtan mi mthun phyogs nyams dang/ /rnam par mi rtog ye shes ldan/ /'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/ /sems can rnam smin
22a4(mdo 'grel): byed rnam gsum/ /shes rab mi mthun phyogs nyams dang/ /rnam bar mi rtog ye shes ldan/ /'dod pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed/ /sems can rnam smin byed rnam gsum/ /snga ma la rten phyi ma skye/ /dman dang mchog tu gnas phyir dang/ /rags pa dang ni phra ba'i phyir/ /de dag rim par
22a5(mdo 'grel): bstan ba yin/ /dbul ba 'dor bar byed pa dang/ /bsil ba 'thong dang khro bzod dang/ /mchog sbyor ba dang yid 'dzin dang/ /don dam shes pa'i phyir bshad do/ /thams cad sgom ba dngos po dang/ /de bzhin yid la byed pa dang/ /bsem pa dang ni thabs dag dang/ /dbang 'byor
22a6(mdo 'grel): nyid la rten pa brjod/ /don rnams btod par byed pa dang/ /rtsa ba sems pa la brten dang/ /lus dang longs spyod phun tshogs dang/ /gnyis rjes 'dzin dang rdzogs byed dang/ /de yang ser sna med ldan dang/ /chos dang zang zing mi 'jigs gtong/ /sbyin pa de 'dor yongs shes
22a7(mdo 'grel): nas/ /mkhas pa yang dag sgrub par byed/ /yan lag drug zhi bsam pas zin/ /bde 'gro gnas ba sbyin byed dang/ /rten dang zhi dang 'jigs ba med/ /bsod nams tshogs dang ldan ba dang/ /?  brtags chos nyid thob pa ste/ /sdom la gnas pa rnams la yod/ /tshul khrim
22b1(mdo 'grel): de 'drar yongs shes nas/ /mkhas pa yang dag sgrub par byed/ /mi mjed ji mi snyam pa dang/ /snying rje chos la brten pa'i phyir/ /phan yon lngar ni yang dag bshad/ /de ni nyid kyi don byed de/ /dka' thub gtso dang kun tu ldan/ /de la de ni rnam gsum 'dod/ /bzod pa de 'drar yongs shes nas/ mi bas ?
22b2(mdo 'grel): dag sgrub par byed/ /dge la yang dag spro ba dang/ /dad dang 'dun la brten pa dang/ /dran sogs yon tan 'phel byed dang/ /kun nas nyon mongs gnyen po dang/ /ma chags la sogs yon tan ldan/ /de dag la ni de rnam bdun/ /brtson 'grub de 'drar yongs shes nas/ /mkhas pa
22b3(mdo 'grel): yang dag sgrub par byed/ /sems ni nang du gnas pa dang/ /dran dang brtson 'grus la brten pa/ /bde ba skyed par byed pa dang/ /mngon shes gnas la dbang bsgyur ba/ /chos rnams kyi ni gtso bo ste/ /de dag la yod de rnam gsum/ /bsam gtan de 'drar yongs shes nas/ /mkhas pa yang
22b4(mdo 'grel): dag sgrub par byed/ /shes bya yang dag rab rnam 'byed/ /ting nge 'dzin la brten pa dang/ /kun nas nyon mongs shin tu grol/ /shes rab 'tsho ba legs bshad dang/ /chos rnams kyi ni mchog yin te/ /de dag la yod de rnam gsum/ /shes rab de 'drar yongs shes nas/ /mkhas pa
22b5(mdo 'grel): yang dag sgrub par byed/ /dkar po'i chos kun rnam par g.yeng ba dang/ /mnyam par bzhag dang gnyis kar shes par bya/ /pha rol phyin pa gnyis dang gnyis/ /gnyis kyis yongs su bsdus pa yin/ /byang chub sems dpa' i sbyin pa ni/ /ma chags mi chags chags ba med/ /chags
22b6(mdo 'grel): pa nyid kyang ma yin te/ /ma chags mi chags chags pa med/ /byang chub sems dpa' i tshul khrims ni/ /ma chags mi chags ma chags pa med/ /chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/ /ma chags mi chags chags ba med/ /byang chub sems dpa' i bzod pa ni/ /ma chags mi chags chags
22b7(mdo 'grel): pa med/ /chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/ /ma chags mi chags chags pa med/ /byang chub sems dpa' i brtson 'grus ni/ /ma chags mi chags chags pa med/ /chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/ /ma chags mi chags chags pa med/ /byang chub sems dpa' i bsam gtan ni//
23a1(mdo 'grel): ma chags mi chags chags pa med/ /chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/ /ma chags mi chags chags pa med/ /byang chub sems dpa' i shes rab ni/ /ma chags mi chags chags ba med/ chags pa nyid kyang ma yin te/ /ma chags mi chags chags pa med/ /sangs rgyas sras rnams
23a2(mdo 'grel): slong dang brad na rang gi srog kyang rtag tu btong/ /snying rjes gzhan la lan kyang mi re 'dod pa'i 'bras bu don mi gnyer/ /sbyin pa de nyid kyis kyang skye bo thams cad byang chub gsum la bkod/ /sbyin pa ye shes kyis yongs zin pas 'jig rten dag na mi zad//
23a3(mdo 'grel): bzhag /sangs rgyas sras rnams sdom dang brtson pa'i rang bzhin tshul khrims gsum rtags blangs/ /mtho ris mngon pa mi 'dod yang dag thob kyang de la chags mi skyed/ /tshul khrims de nyid kyis kyang skye bo thams cad byang chub gsum la bkod/ /tshul khrims ye shes
23a4(mdo 'grel): kyis yongs zin pas 'jig rten dag na mi zad bzhag/ sangs rgyas sras rnams shin tu bya dka' de bzhin mi yi gnod kun bzod/ /mtho ris gnyer dang mi nus bas min 'jigs pas ma min par rtas min/ /bzod pa bla na med pas skye bo thams cad byang chub
23a5(mdo 'grel): gsum la bkod/ /bzod pa ye shes kyis yongs zin pas 'jig rten dag na mi zad bzhag/ sangs rgyas sras rnams go cha sbyor ba'i bdag nyid brtson 'grus dpe med byas/ /rang dang gzhan gyi nyon mongs tshogs gzhom byang chub dam pa 'thob bar byed/ /brtson 'grus
23a6(mdo 'grel): de nyid kyis kyang skye bo thams cad byang chub gsum la bkod/ /brtson 'grus ye shes kyis yongs zin pas 'jig rten dag na mi bzad bzhag/ sangs rgyas sras rnams ting 'dzin mang ldan bsam gtan rnam pa thams cad bsgrubs/ /bsam gtan bde ba
23a7(mdo 'grel): phul gyis gnas shing snying rjes skye ba dman la rton/ /bsam gtan de nyid kyang ni skye bo thams cad byang chub gsum la bkod/ /bsam gtan ye shes kyis yongs zin pas 'jig rten dag na mi bzad bzhag/ sangs rgyas sras rnams de nyid shes bya gang yin
23b1(mdo 'grel): mdza' dag rnam kun shes/ /mya ngan 'das la'ang blo yis chags rab ma tre? skyed 'khor bar smos ci dgos/ /ye shes de nyid kyis kyang skye bo thams cad byang chub gsum la bkod/ /ye shes sems can yongs su bzung bas 'jig rten dag na mi bzang bzhag/ rgya che ba dang zad
23b2(mdo 'grel): zid med/ /don che ba dang mi zad pa/ /sbyin pa la sogs thams cad kyi/ /yon tan bzhir ni shes par bya/ /slong ba mthong rdzogs dga' ba dang/ /mi dga' ba dang smon pa yang/ /sbyin pa de ni brtser ldan pas/ /lhag par ldan pas rtag zil gnon/ /brtse bas sems can rnams
23b3(mdo 'grel): la ni/ /srog dang longs spyod chung ma dag/ rtag gtong shin tu dga' byed pa/ /de spong ji ltar srung mi 'gyur/ /'phags pa mi lta sems snyoms shing/ /mi 'jigs brtse phyir kun ster ba/ /gzhan la gnod pa byed pa yi/ /logs pa'i tshig ni ji ltar smra/ /snyoms par phan par
23b4(mdo 'grel): 'dod pa brtse ba can/ /gzhan gyi sdug bsngal skye bas shin tu 'jigs/ /sems can 'dul ba la ni legs brtson pa/ /ngag gi nyes rnams gsum las shin tu ring/ /thams cad btong ba snying rje can/ /rten 'byung chos la rab mkhas pa/ de ni yid kyi nyon mongs kun/ /ji lta bur
23b5(mdo 'grel): na dang du len/ /brtser ldan gang tshe gnod par byed pa dang/ /gzhan la phan pa'i sdug bsngal la brtags du/ /phan pa'i 'du shes dga' brnyed 'gyur ba/ /de yis gang la ci zhig bzod par bya/ /gzhan la gzhan gyi 'du shes bral ba dang/ /bdag pas ches lhag gzhan la brtag
23b6(mdo 'grel): byams dang/ /bka' ba spyod phyir brtse ba dang bcas la/ /brtson 'grus bka' ba min la shin tu bka' / /gsum gyi bsam gtan bde ba chung/ /bdag bde zhen bar yongs su 'gyur/ /zad 'gyur rmongs dang bcas bar 'dod/ /byang chub sems dpa' i bzlog pa'o/ /ji ltar
23b7(mdo 'grel): mtshan mo lag nom dang/ /khebs spron de bzhin shes pas gsum/ /snying rje can gyi shes pa ni/ /nyi ma'i zer bzhin mtshungs pa med/ /sbyin pa brten dang gzhi dang ni/ /rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang/ /rgyu dang ye shes zhing dag dang/ gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu
24a1(mdo 'grel): 'dod/ /tshul khrims brten dang bzhi dang ni/ /rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang/ /rgyu dang ye shes zhing ngag dang/ /gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/ /bzod pa brten dang bzhid ste/ /rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang/ /rgyu dang ye shes zhing dga' ba
24a2(mdo 'grel): gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/ /brtson 'grus brten dang gzhi dang ni/ /rgyu mtshan ngang ni yongs sngo dang/ /rgyu dang ye shes zhing dag dang/ /gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/ bsam gtan rten dang gzhi dang ni/ /rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang/ /rgyu dang
24a3(mdo 'grel): ye shes zhing dag dang/ /gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/ /shes rab rten dang gzhi dang ni/ rgyu mtshon dang ni yongs bsngo dang/ /rgyu dang ye shes zhing dag dang/ /gnas kyi sgo nas mchog tu 'dod/ /byang chub sems dpa' i sbyin pa ni/ /sems can gcig
24a4(mdo 'grel): bde bskal ma du/ /gnod pa byed kyang dgar 'gyur na/ /de las bzlog pa smros ci dgos/ lus can rnams ni gang phyir nor 'dod pa/ /brtan rnams de nyid lus can rnams la gtong/ /sye'o? rnams ni lus phyir nor 'dod de/ /de nyid brtan rnams rgya phrag rnams
24a5(mdo 'grel): su btod/ /gang tshe lus nyid btod yang yid stag mi bsngal ba de tshe rdzas ngan lta la smos kyang ci zhig dgos/ /de 'di'i 'jig rten 'das pa de 'dis dga' 'gyur ba/ /gang de ni de'i yang bla ma yin/ /ji ltar blo ldan 'di ni kun btong bas/ /don
24a6(mdo 'grel): gnyer skye bo dga' bas dga' ba ltar/ /de ltar slongs mo bdag blang bya ba/ /'dod dgu thob pa dag gis dga' mi 'gyur/ /blo ldan bdog? dgu btang bas nod med pa/ /bdag nyid nor ldan sems pa ji lta bar/ /slang ba longs spyod kun rdzogs bdag nyid ni/ /de ltar nod dang
24a7(mdo 'grel): ldan par mi sme so/ /ji ltar blo ldan 'di ni sbyin pa bzang po chul bzhin du/ don gnyer tshim byas de la phan cher 'dogs par sems pa ltar/ /de bzhin slangs? ma bdag shin tu nod mang thob nas ni/ /sbyin pa po la rnyad pa'i rgyu yis drin du mi rtsi'o/ /lam ka'i? 'bras?
24b1(mdo 'grel): mchog ldan pa'i longs spyod shing las ji lta bar/ /lus can rnams kyis gang gi nor rdzas rgya chen blangs nas ni/ /bdag nyid dogs dang bral bar rang nyams spong par byed pa la/ /btang dga' longs spyod can de byang chub sems dpa' las gzhan min/ /gtso dang de rgya
24b2(mdo 'grel): las kyis dbye ba dang/ rnam pa'i dbye brten gyis dbye ba dang/ /bar chad rnam gzhi'i gnyen po'i dbye ba yis/ /brtson 'grus yongs shes bya zhes rab tu bstan/ /dge ba'i tshogs gyi nang na brtson 'grus mchog/ /'di ltar de la brten nas de rjes thob/ /brtson 'grus kyis ni mong
24b3(mdo 'grel): la bde gnas mchog/ /dngos grub 'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten gtogs/ /brtson 'grus kyis ni srid sbyor 'dod pa thob/ /brtson 'grus gyis ni dag par rab 'gyur ldan/ /brtson 'grus gyis ni 'jig rten 'das nas grol/ /brtson 'grus kyis ni byang chub mchog sangs
24b4(mdo 'grel): rgyas/ /gzhan yang mnyam dang 'phel ba'i brtson 'grus dang/ /thar pa'i dbang dang mi mthun phyogs spangs gzhan/ /de nyid rab zhugs yongs su sgyur byed dang/ /brtson 'grus don chen des tshig gzhan du 'dod/ /thog mar ga tshi'i? brtson 'grus de nas ni/ /'tshul bzhin
24b5(mdo 'grel): rab zhugs sbyor ba'i brtson 'grus te/ /ma zhum mi 'khrugs chog mi shes brtson 'grus/ /rnam pa thams cad sangs rgyas rnams rab gsung/ /theg pa gsum brtson skye bo la brtan nas/ /bsam blo zhan dang rgya rab che ldan phyir/ /brtson 'grus tha ma 'bring dang
24b6(mdo 'grel): mchog gzhan te/ /de ni don chung ba dang don chen 'dod/ /brtson 'grus ldan pa longs spyod kyis pham med/ /brtson 'grus ldan pa nyon mongs kyis pham med/ /brtson 'grus ldan pa skyo bas pham pa med/ /brtson 'grus ldan pa thob pas bam pa med/ /phan tshun
24b7(mdo 'grel): bsdus pa phyir rab dbye'i phyir/ /chos nyid phyir dang rgyu mtshan phyir/ /pha rol phyin drug rnam kun tu/ /rnam par nges par shes par bya/ /sbyir mtshungs de ston len 'jug dang/ /bdag nyid rjes 'jug rnams kyis/ /snyan par smra dang don spyod dang/ /don mthun nyid du 
25a1(mdo 'grel): 'dod pa yin/ /phan par byed pa'i thabs dang ni/ /'dzin pa byed dang 'jug byed dang/ de bzhin rjes su 'jug byed pa/ bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhir shes bya/ /dang pos snod 'gyur dngos po ste/ gnyis pa yis ni mos pa yin/ /gsum pa yis na sdug?
25a2(mdo 'grel): pa ste/ /bzhi pas rnam par sbyong ba'o/ /zang zing dang ni chos kyis te/ /dmigs pa chos la sogs pa yis/ /bsdu ba gnyis kyis sgo nas ni/ /bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhing 'dod do/ /rnam pa'i dbye pa'i sgo nas ni/ bsdu? ba dman dang 'bring dang mchog/ phal cher don med don
25a3(mdo 'grel): dang/ /rnam kun don yod shes par bya/ /'khor spung pa dang ldan pa rnams/ /tshul 'di la ni yang dag brten/ /kun gyi don kun sgrub byed cing/ /thabs bzang yin par rab tu sngags/ /bsdud dang sdud par 'gyur ba dang/ /gang dag da ltar sdud byed pa/ /de kun de 'dra de lta
25a4(mdo 'grel): bas/ /'di ni sems can smin byed lam/ /de ltar rtag tu long spyod ma chags blo/ /zhi sdom brtson pa'i pha rol phyin gnas bdag/ srid yul mtshan ma rnam par mi rtog pa/ /de ni sems can tshogs sdud byed pa yin/ /pha rol tu phyin pa'i skabs rdzogs so//
25a5(mdo 'grel): rab dang sems dang ldan pa yis/ /tshogs gnyis rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir/ /sangs rgyas rnams la gos sogs kyis/ /mngon sum mngon sum min par 'chad/ /sangs rgyas 'byung ba don yod par/ /smon lam dang ni ldan pa yis/ /gsum po dmigs
25a6(mdo 'grel): par mi byed pa/ /sangs rgyas mchod pa rdzogs pa yin/ /sems can dag ni tshad med pa/ /yongs su smin bar byed pa gzhan/ /rdzas dang sems kyi sgro nas gzhan/ /mos ba dang ni smon pa dang/ /brtse dang yongs dag dang ni/ /yang dag sbyod pa'i sgo dang ni//
25a7(mdo 'grel): gzhid la gtong dang rtog pa dang/ /grol dang de bzhin nyid kyis gzhan/ /rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang/ /rten dang dang po dang rgyu dang ni/ /ye shes dang ni zhing dag dang/ /gnas kyi mchod pa rab bstan pa? rgyu dang 'bras bu nyid dang ni/ /bdag nyid dang
25b1(mdo 'grel): ni bzhan ngag dang/ rnyed dang bkur sti nyid dang ni/ /sgrub ba'i sgo nas nga rnam gnyis/ /mchod pa cung dang chen po ste/ /nga rgyal bcas dang nga rgyal med/ /sbyor dang 'gro ba nyid dang ni/ /smon pa'i sgo nas der 'dod do/ /rang gi sems kyis sangs rgyas rnam mchod pa//
25b2(mdo 'grel): chos la mos dang bsam dang dbang 'byor dang/ /rnam par mi rtog thabs yongs bzung ba dang/ /kun nas don gcig nyid la 'jug pas mchog/ /rten pa rten dang gzhi dang ni/ /rgyu mtshan dang ni yongs bsngo dang/ /rgyu dang ye shes zhing dag dang/ /gnas gyi sgo nas rab tu
25b3(mdo 'grel): bstan/ /ba shes gnyen dul ba zhi zhing nyer bzhi pa/ /yon tan lhag pa brtson bcas lung gis phyug/ de nyid rab tu rtogs pa smra mkhas ldan/ /brtse ba'i bdag nyid skyo ba spangs? la brten/ /bkur sti brnyed pa dag dang rim go dang/ /sgrub ba'i sgo nas bshes gtan
25b4(mdo 'grel): brten par bya ? bsten gzhi de bzhin blo ldan chos la ni/ /shes bsam dus su 'dud pas bshes gnyen bgrod/ /de ni bsnyen bkur rnyed la 'dod/ pa me ba/ bsgrub bar bya phyir ? yongs su bsngo bar byed/ /bsten pa ji skad bstan pa bsgrub pa des/ /de yi sems ni yang
25b5(mdo 'grel): dag mgu bar byed/ /theg pa gsum la mkhas pa blo rtogs nas/ /rang gi theg pa 'grub par bya phyir 'bad/ /sems can tshad med yongs smin bya phyir dang/ /zhing dag pa yang sbyar bar bya ba'i phyir/ /de chos bag bskal la sbyod yon tan ldan/ bshes
25b6(mdo 'grel): gnyen rab tu sten byed zang zing min/ /blo dang ldan pa rgyu dang 'bras bu dang/ /chos sgo rjes 'gro phyi dang thos mnyan dang/ /sems kyi rnam 'byor nga rgyal bcas pa dang/ /nga rgyal med yid ldan bas bshes gnyen bstan/ /blo ldan 'gro dang sbyor ba dang/ /smon pa'i sgo nas bsheS
25b7(mdo 'grel): gnyen sten/ /rang gi sems kyis bshes gnyen mchog sten pa/ /chos la mos dang bsam dang dbang 'byor dang/ /rnam par mi rtog thabs yongs bzung ba dang/ /kun dang don gcig nyid la 'jug pas mchog/ bstan pa'i tshangs pa mi mthun slangs/ /rnam par mi rtog ye
26a1(mdo 'grel): shes ldan/ /dmigs pa rnam pa gsum la 'jug/ /sems can rnams ni yongs smin byed/ /brtan pa rnams kyi de dag bde 'dod dang/ /sdug bsngal gyis nyam thag dang bde ba dang/ /nyon mongs can dang de dag bstan bcos dang/ /de yi de bzhin
26a2(mdo 'grel): nyid la rab tu 'jug de don de bzhin nyid phyir dang/ /zhib thob brang ? phyir dang/ /las gnyis bas? nyon mongs zad pI phyir/ phyis ba dmigs pa med pa yin/ /de dag g.yo dang mi g.yo dang/ /chags pas ro nyam min zhes bya/ /byang chub sems dpa' mi gyod/ /chags dang bral bas rab tu gnas
26a3(mdo 'grel): mnyam bzhag ngo bo nyid min chung/ /'bring dang dman pa'i sa pa dang/ /bsam pa dman dang nga rgyal bcas/ /gang yin de dman gzhan nyid lhag/ tshangs pa'i gnas pas gnas pa yi/ /blo ldan rtag tu 'dod par skye/ /des ni tshogs rnams rdzogs byed cing/ /sems can
26a4(mdo 'grel): dag kyang rnam smin byed/ /kun tu tshangs dang mi 'bral la/ /de yi mi mthun phyogs dang bral/ /bag med gyur kyang de yi rkyen/ /mi bzang bas kyang mi 'gyur ro/ /byang chub sems dpa' gnod sems dang/ /rnam 'tshe mi dga' gnod sems dang/ /'dod pa'i 'dod chags dang
26a5(mdo 'grel): ldan pa/ /nyes dmigs rnam pa mang la dag/ nyon mongs kyis ni bdag 'joms sems can 'jams shing tshul khrims 'joms/ /nyams bcas rnyad? bas dman zhing srung dang de bzhin stan pas smod?/ /brtsod bcas mi snyan de'i gzhan du mi khom rnams su skye/ /thob
26a6(mdo 'grel): dang ma thob nyams pas yid la sdug bsngal chen po 'thob/ /nyes pa 'di kun byams sogs la/ /legs par gnas lam 'byung ste/ /nyon mongs can min sems can gyis don du'i 'khor ba'ang yongs mi btong/ /ji ltar rgyal pa'i sras rnams
26a7(mdo 'grel): sems can la/ /byams pa la sogs sems pa 'di 'byung pa'i/ /sems can thams cad yon tan ldan pa yi/ /bu gcig pa la'ang de lta ma yin 'o/ /rab 'bar dgra yi dbang du sang/ /sdug bsngal gyis non mun pas bsgrig /'grong dkyil? la kun tu zhugs/
26b1(mdo 'grel): 'ching ba che dang yang dag ldan/ /zas chen dug dang 'dres la zhen/ /lam ni rab tu stor gyur pa/ /lam gol rab zhugs stobs chung ba'i/ /sems can rnams la snying rje'o/ /'tshe srangs byang chub mchog gi sa bon dang/ /bde ba bskyed dang gdung byed 'dod pa'i rgyu/ /ngo bo nyid spin chos
26b2(mdo 'grel): la brten pa yi/ /rgyal ba'i sras la byang chub thag mi ring/ /snying rje blo mchog 'khor bar gtogs pa yi/ /sdug bsngal bdag nyid kun dang bdag med pa'ang/ /rnam pa shes nas skyo bar mi 'gyur zhing/ /nyes bas rab gnad bar lnga mi 'gyur ro/ /'jig rten sdug bsngal
26b3(mdo 'grel): bdag nyid lta ba yi/ /brtse dang ldan pas sdug bsngal de dang ni/ /de yongs spangs pa'i thabs kyang ji bzhin rib/ /nyam nga bar byed skyo bar yang mi 'gyur/ /snying rje'i bdag nyid can gyi brtse ba 'di/ /rang bzhin dang ni so sor rtogs ba dang/ /de sngon goms par byas dang ldan pa
26b4(mdo 'grel): dang/ /mi mthun phyogs nyams rnam dag thob pa bzhi/ /mnyam dan rtag med lhag pa'i bsam pas min/ /sgrub pa'i sgo nas 'dod chags bral ba dang/ /mi dmigs bas min gang ba brtse min te/ /de bzhin brdza med gang de byang chub min/ /snying rje dang ni bzod dang sems pa
26b5(mdo 'grel): dang/ /smon lam skye ba sems can yongs smin byed/ /dang bo rtsa ba tha ma 'bras mchog ldan/ /'di ni snying rje'i ljon shing chen po yin/ /rtsa ba snying rje med gyur na/ /dka' spyod bzod pa nyid mi 'gyur/ /blo ldan sdug bsngal mi bzod na/ /sems can don sems nyid mi 'gyur//
26b6(mdo 'grel): sems pa dang ni bral ba'i blo/ /skye ba dkar po rnam dag tu/ /smon lam? 'debs bar mi 'gyur ro/ /skye ba bzang po ma thob na/ /sems can yongs smin byed mi 'gyur/ /snying rje'i mchu ba byams ba ste/ /de sdug bsngal na bde ba yis/ /yangs rgyas tshul bzhin yid/ byed bas/ /yan
26b7(mdo 'grel): lag rgya chen 'phel ba dang/ /smon lam rgyun ni ma bcad pas/ /lo ma 'dor len rkyen rnams gnyis/ thub pa de phyir me tog dang/ /'bras bu dron yor? shes par bya/ /snying rje chen po yon tan 'byung gnas kyi/ /sems can rnams la snying rjes su mi byed/ /'di ltar 'di
27a1(mdo 'grel): dag la ni sdug bsngal yang/ /brtses bskyed bde ba gzhal du med pa 'byung/ /snying rje zin pa'i brtse ldan rnams/ /zhi la 'ang yid ni mi gnas na/ /'jig rten bde dang rang srog la/ /chags par 'gyur ba smos ci dgos/ /kha na ma tho med pa'i byams
27a2(mdo 'grel): pa gang/ /de ni yod min 'jig rten pa yang yin/ /blo ldan rnams kyi rtse bas byams ba ni/ /kha nama tho med cing 'jig rten 'das/ /sdug bsngal dpa' brgal che dang mi shes pa'i/ /mun pa chel brten par gyur pa yi/ /'jig rten 'dren pa'i thabS gang yin pa de/ /ji ltar kha na
27a3(mdo 'grel): mtho med mi 'gyur/ /'jig rten byang chub rang sangs rgyas pa yis/ /dgra bcom rnams la byams pa de med na/ /de las gzhan la smos kyang ci dgos pa// ji ltar 'jig rten 'das pa ma yin 'gyur/ /byang chub sems dpa' sdug bsngal med/ /brtebs sdug bsngal
27a4(mdo 'grel): 'gyur ba gang/ /de la dang por kun tu sbag/ reg nas shin tu mngon bar dga' / /brtse bas bskyed pa'i sdug bsngal 'jig rten gyi/ /bde ba thams cad zil gyis gnon 'gyur zhing/ /don byas rnams kyang de dang mi ldan gang/ /de las ngo mtshar che ba ci zhig yod/ bstan pa'i
27a5(mdo 'grel): brtse dang ldan pa'i sbyin pa yis/ /sbyin pa'i bde ba byed pa gang yin pa/ /de la khams gsum nye bar spyad rnams kyi/ /bde bde yis chang yang mi 'phong ngo/ /sems can don phyir brtse bas sdug bsngal gyi/ /rang bzhin 'khor ba gang yin mi btong na/ /snying rje can rnams
27a6(mdo 'grel): gzhan la phan pa'i phyir/ /sdug bsngal ci ste khas len byed mi 'gyur/ /brtse dang ldan pa'i snying rje'i sbyin pa dang/ /longs spyod dang ni de las byams pa dang/ /rjes su bzung bas bskyed dang de yi mthus/ /byas pa'i bde ba'i rtag tu 'phel bar 'gyur/ /snying rje rgyas par bya zhing
27a7(mdo 'grel): 'phel bar bya/ /sbyin la yongs smin bya zhing bde bar bya/ /kun tu drang bar bya zhi bkri bya zhes/ /zhen pa rnams la rab tu smra dang 'dra/ /snying rjes sdug bsngal ngag gis sdug bsngal ba/ /bde ma bskyed par gang gis bde bar 'gyur/ /de phyir brtse dang ldan pas gzhan bde ga/
27b1(mdo 'grel): bskyed nas bdag nyid bde bar byed pa yin/ /snying rje can ni rtag tu rang spyin la/ /ston dang 'dra ste rang bde mi 'dod pa/ /longs spyod rnams kyis gzhan dag bde bar gyis/ /yang na tha dang min bde bdag lang min/ /de bde sa bde ba bdag gis sbyin pa ni/ /'bras dang bces te
27b2(mdo 'grel): sems can rnams la byin/ /gal te khyod kyis bdag la bya ba yod/ /de dag nyid la shin tu 'bras bus byos/ /sbyin pa po ni longs spyod mi 'dod kyang/ /longs spyod shin tu mang la bzang dang 'phrad/ /bdag ni bde bde 'dod ma yin te/ /'di ltar bdag ni sbyin la brgyud dang ldan/ /
27b3(mdo 'grel): bdag ni rtag tu brtse bas bdog pa kun/ /yongs su btong ba gang yin de ltos la/ /de nas khyod kyis bdag na di 'bris la/ /don gnyer med pa nyid du shes par bya/ /gal te khyod 'bras thob pa mi btod na/ /sbyin la mngon dga' yin par mi 'gyur te/ /'di ltar skad cig tsam yang
27b4(mdo 'grel): sbyin med na/ /sbyin la mngon par dga' ba nyid ma yin/ /ma byas pa la 'bras bu mi 'byin te/ /'di ltar lan bltas bdag gi cha ma yin/ /khyod kyi lan la lta dang bral bas na/ /'bras bu shin tu gzhan la gtong ba yin/ /rgyal sras rnams kyi brtse bas sbyin pa ni/ kha na mtho
27b5(mdo 'grel): med cing dag ba'i bzhi/ /bde bar 'dron bar byed pa nyid dang ni/ /rjes su bsrung bcas tshol med dgos pa med/ /rgyal sras rnams kyi brtsa bas sbyin ba ni/ /mdza' dag rgya chen gtso dang rtag pa dang/ /dga' dang zang zing med dang dag pa dang/ /byang chub la gzhol dag la gzhol ba yin
27b6(mdo 'grel): ji ltar bde ba gsum gyis tsham pa'i yid/ /brtse ldan yongs su btang bas dga' 'gyur ba/ /longs spyod can dag nye bar spyad pa yis/ /de ltar dga' bar 'gyur ba ma yin no/ /bkren la brtse dang ma rungs pa la brtse/ /kun 'khrul la brtse bag med rnams la brtse//
27b7(mdo 'grel): yul gyi bzhan dbang can la brtse ba dang/ /khog par mngon par zhen la snying rje'o/ /bde dang sdug bsngal de rgyu las/ /byang chub sems dpa' i snying rje ste/ /rgyu dang bshes gnyen ? bzhin las/ /byang chub sems dpa' i snying rje'i/ /byang chub sems dpa' i snying rje ni/ /mnyam
28a1(mdo 'grel): par shes ? de bsam phyir/ sgrub phyir 'dod chags bral phyir dang/ /mi dmigs phyir dang dag phyir ro/ /rang gi sems kyis byams la sogs/ /sgom pa chos la mos pa dang/ /bsam dang dbang 'byor nyid dang ni/ /rnam par mi rtog gcig
28a2(mdo 'grel): phyir mchog/ de ltar bcom ldan 'das la dang bar ba skyes shes?/ /rdzas dang bkur sti chen pos shin tu rgyun mchod ldan/ /yon tan mang ldan phan bde bshes la rtag rten pa/ /'gro la rjes su brtse ba grub pa kun thob 'gyur/ /mchod pa dang brten pa dang tshad
28a3(mdo 'grel): med pa'i skabs rdzogs so// //ngo tsha mi mthun phyogs spangs dang/ /rnam pa mi rtog ye shes ldan/ /kha na ma tho med dman yul/ sems can smin byed bstan pa'i yin/ /pha rol phyin pa drug pa yis/ /mi mthun phyogs ni 'phel ba dang//
28a4(mdo 'grel): gnyen po 'grib pas byang chub sems/ /mi bzang ngo tsha skye bar 'gyur/ /brtan rnams pha rol phyin pa drub/ /bsten pa la ni le lo dang/ /nyon mongs rjes su mthun chos la/ /sbyor ba las kyang ngo mtshar 'gyur/ /mnyam gzhag ngo bo nyid min chung/ /'brid dang
28a5(mdo 'grel): dman pa'i sa ba dang/ /bsam pa dman dang ngar? bcas pa'i/ /ngo tshad man de las gzhan lhag/ blo ldan ngo tsha med pa ni/ /tshul bzhin min bas nyon mongs dag/ dad du len zhing khong khro dang/ /yal bar 'dor dang nga rgyal gyis/ /sems can rnams dang tshul
28a6(mdo 'grel): khrims 'joms/ /'gyod pas nyams dang bcas 'gyur zhing/ /bkur sti dman pa 'thob 'gyur des/ /dang ldan mi min tshogs dang ni/ /ston pas kyang ni btang snyoms mdzad/ /rgyal sras chos dang mthun rnams kyis /rnam par smod cing 'jig rten las/
28a7(mdo 'grel): mthun rnams kyis /rnam par smod cing 'jig rten laS// khom skye/ /de na chos dkar thob pa dang/ /mthob pa las rnams nyams 'gyur/ /de phyir sdug bsngal gnaS pa dang/ yid kyang rnal du mi gnas 'gyur/ /rgyal sras ngo tsha ldan rnams la/ /nyes pa'i
28b1(mdo 'grel): dag kun mi 'byung/ /mkhas pa rtag tu lta dag dang/ /mi rnams su ni yang dag skye/ /blo ldan ngo tshas myur du ni/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub tshogs rdzogs byed/ /rgyal ba'i sras ni sems can rnams/ /smin byed skyo bar mi bsgyur nyid/ /de dag mi mthun phyogs dang ni/ /gnyen po 'bral dang
28b2(mdo 'grel): mi 'bral 'gyur/ /de ltar rgyal sras ngo tsha ldan/ /phan yon de dag thob par 'gyur/ /byis ba shin tu gos bzang gyon yang ni/ /khrel dang bral phyir nyes pa'i dri ma can/ /rgyal sras ngo tsha shes pa'i gos can ni/ /dga' ba med kyang nyes pa'i dri ma bral/ /rgyal ba'i sras ni
28b3(mdo 'grel): khrel dang ldan gyur ba/ /nam mkha' bzhin du chos kyis mi gos 'gyur/ /rgyal sras rnams kyi nang du 'dus gyur pa/ /ngo tsha shes pas brgyan pa mdzes pa yin/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni ngo tsha bas/ /gdul bya rnams la ma bzhin byams pa nyid/ /ngo tsha ba ni nyes pa
28b4(mdo 'grel): thams cad las/ /'khor pa kun tu bsrung bar byed pa'ang yin/ /kun la dang du len pa dang/ /kun la dang du mi len zhing/ /kun la mi 'jug 'jug pa ni/ /khrel ldan khrel bas byas pa'i rtagS/ rang gis sems kyis khrel sgo pa/ /chos la mos dang bsam pa dang//
28b5(mdo 'grel): dbang 'byor ba dang mi rtog dang/ /gcig pa nyid kyis gtso bo yin/ /byang chub sems dpa' i bstan pa ni/ /de las gzhan pa thams cad las/ /mtshan nyid dang ni rab dbye dang/ /mi 'gyur bas ni khyad par 'phags/ /brtson 'grus ting 'dzin shes rab ni/ /snying stobs
28b6(mdo 'grel): sran thub brtan par 'dod/ /gang phyir gsum gyis byang chub sems/ /'jigs pa med par rab tu 'jug/ zhum dang g.yo dang rmongs pa yis/ /bya ba rnams la 'jigs pa skye/ /de phyir gnyug ma gsum la ni/ /bstan pa'i ming du shes par bya/ /rang bzhin dang ni smon
28b7(mdo 'grel): lam dang/ /lta ba med ba nyid dang ni/ /sems can log par sgrub pa dang/ /zab cing rgya che thos pa dang/ /gdul bya 'dul bar dka' ba dang/ /rgyal sku bsam gyis mi khyab dang/ /bka' ba dag ni sna tshogs pa dang/ /'khor ba gtong ba med pa nyid/ /de nyid nyon mongs ba med?
29a1(mdo 'grel): med pa la/ /brtan pa'i bstan bskye ba ni/ /de las gzhan dang mi mtshungs te/ /brtan rnams kyi ni mchog tu 'dod/ /phye ma 'kho dang 'dod chags dang/ /rgya mtsho dag gis ri rab star/ /brtan la grogs ngan sdug bsngal dang/ /zab mo thos pas
29a2(mdo 'grel): mi g.yos so/ /byang chub mi skyo mnyam med pa/ /bzhi gsum thos pas mi doms dang/ /brtson 'grus tshe dang sdug bsngal la/ /khrel dang bstan la bsten pa ste/ /byang chub che la 'dun ba drag /blo ldan rnam kyi mi skyo ba/ /sa rnams la ni ma rdzogs dang/ /rdzogs dang shin tu
29a3(mdo 'grel): rdzogs par 'dod/ /brtan pa'i bstan bcos shes pa nyid/ /bzhi dang ched du bya ba dang/ las dang mtshan nyid dag dang ni/ /mi bzang nyid dang 'bras bu ni/ /yang dag 'grub pas khyad par 'phags/ /ting nge 'dzin dang bzungs sgos bsdus/ /sems can smin bar byed pa dang
29a4(mdo 'grel): dam chos 'dzin bar byed pa yin/ /bstan rnams 'jig rten shes pa nyid/ /lus dang ngag yid dag dang ni/ /bden pa shes pas mnyam pa med/ /de las gzhan pa dag las 'phags/ /brtan rnams rtag tu 'jum par byed/ /gsong po dag tu smra ba yin/ /sems can
29a5(mdo 'grel): snod du bya ba'i phyir/ /dam chos bsgrub par bya ba'i phyir/ /gang phyir bden pa gnyis kyis ni/ /'jig rten rnamS dag 'byung bar 'dod/ /gnyis kyi nub 'gyur de yi phyir/ /de shes 'jig rten shes zhes bya/ /de dag zhi bya thob bya'i phyir/ /blo ldan bden pa rnams las sbyor
29a6(mdo 'grel): gang phyir blo ldan bden shes byir/ /'jig rten shes zhes nges par brjod/ /gtsug lag bstan pa'i chos dang ni/ /de don dgongs pa can dang ni/ /nges don tshad mar ldan pa dang/ /de yi brjod med thob pa'o/ /spong dang ji skad bshad pa dang/ /log par yang dag shes
29a7(mdo 'grel): ba dang/ /brjod dang bcas pa thob pa dag /'dir ni dgag par bstan pa yin/ /mos dang rnam par dpyod pa dang/ /gzhan dang ji bzhin thos pa dang/ /brjod pa med pa'i ye shes las/ /bstan rnams nyams par mi 'gyur ro/ /rnam grangs dang ni mtshan nyid dang/ /
29b1(mdo 'grel): tshig dang ye shes shes pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' i yang dag rig/ bzhi po mtshungs pa med par 'dod/ /bstan pa la ni rab brtson pa'i/ /gang dang gang gis ston pa ni/ /chos dang don ni gnyis po dag/ tshig dang shes pa kha nas ston/ /chos ni bstan dang bshad phyir
29b2(mdo 'grel): dang/ /rnam pa kun tu gnyis thob phyir/ /rgol ba rnams kyi lan 'debs phyir/ /so so yang dag rigs pa bzhi/ /mnyam nyid so so rang rig gnas/ /phyis ni rab tu shes pa yin/ /the tshom thams cad gcod byed pa/ /so so yang dag rig pa brjod/ /byang chub sems dpa' 
29b3(mdo 'grel): rnams kyi tshogs/ /bsod nams ye shes mtshungs pa med/ /gcig gis 'khor par mngon mtho byed/ /gzhan gyis nyon mongs med par 'khor/ /sbyin dang tshul khrims bsod nams kyi/ /tshogs yin shes rab ye shes kyi/ /gsum po gzhan ni gnyis ka ste/ /lnga char yang ni
29b4(mdo 'grel): ye shes tshogs/ /rgyun tu sgom pa thob nas ni/ /dge la yang du yang du sgrub/ /bstan pa'i tshogs gang yin pa de/ /don kun sgrub par byed pa yin/ /'jug dang mtshan mas med pa dang/ /lhun gyis grub par bya ba dang/ /dbang bskur mthar thug bya ba'i phyir/ /bstan rnams tshogs ni
29b5(mdo 'grel): sgrub par byed/ /blo ldan dan pa nye bzhag pa/ /sgom pa rnam pa bcu bzhi yis/ /mtshungs pa med pa'i phyir na de/ /de las gzhan las khyad par 'phags/ /rten dang gnyen po dag dang ni/ /de bzhin du ni 'jug pa dang/ /dmigs pa dang ni yid byed dang/ /thob pas sgoms pa khyad par
29b6(mdo 'grel): 'phags/ /mthun dang rjes su 'jug pa dang/ /yongs su shes dang skye ba dang/ /chen po dang ni mchog nyid dang/ /sgom dang yang dag sgrub bas gzhan/ /bstan pa rnams kyi yang dag spong/ /lus can rnams dang mtshungs pa med/ /dran pa nye bar gzhag pa yi/ /nyes pa rnams kyis
29b7(mdo 'grel): gnyen por bsgom/ /'khor bar nye bar spyad pa dang/ /sgrib pa dag ni dor ba dang/ /yid la byed pa dor ba dang/ /sa rnams la ni 'jug pa dang/ /mtshan ma med bar gnas pa dang/ /lung bstan pa ni thob pa dang/ /sems can rnams yongs su smin bya dang/ /dbang ni bskur bar
30a1(mdo 'grel): bya ba dang/ /zhing rnams dag par bya phyir dang/ /mthar thug nyid du bya ba'i phyir/ /byang chub sems dpa' blo ldan rnams/ /mi mthun phyogs kyi gnyen por sgom/ /'dun pa la ni brten nas su/ /rnal 'byor rgyu mtshan bcas sgom pa/ /yang dag spong ba thams cad
30a2(mdo 'grel): la/ /gnyen po zhes ni nges par brjod/ /brtan pa rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul gyi/ /rkang pa mtshan nyid mchog ldan bzhi/ /bdag nyid dang ni gzhan dag gi/ don kun sgrub pa'i phyir skye'o/ /rten dang rab tu dbye ba dang/ /thabs dang mngon par sgrub pa yis/ /blo ldan rdzu 'phrul rkang pa
30a3(mdo 'grel): rnams/ /rnam pa kun tu rnam bzhag 'dod/ /bsam gtan pha rol phyin brten nas/ /rab tu dbye ba dag dang thabs/ /rnam bzhi'i mngon bar sgrub pa ni/ /rnam pa drug du brjod pa yin/ /gcig ni 'bad par byed pa ste/ /gnyis pa 'phan 'dogs bdag nyid yin/ /gsum pa
30a4(mdo 'grel): gtod par byed pa ste/ /bzhi ba gnyen po pa yin no/ /mthong ba dang na gdams ngag dang/ /gnas pa rnam par brtse ba dang/ /smon lam dang ni dbang ngag dang/ /chos thob ba ni sgrub pa'i phyir/ /byang chub spyod dang thos mchog dang/ /zhi gnas lhag mthong dang sogs kyi/ /
30a5(mdo 'grel): gzhi yin par ni shes bya ste/ /don grub byed ba'i skabs kyis so/ /dang sogs sa la 'jus pa ste/ /kun nas nyon mongs can du 'dod/ /mi mthun phyogs nyams chung bas yang/ /de dag nyid la stobs shes bya/ /sar zhugs pa la byang chub kyi/ /yan lag rnaM par gzhag
30a6(mdo 'grel): par brjod/ /chos rnams dang ni sems can kun/ /mnyam pa nyid du rtogs phyir ro/ /shes bya ma rgyal rgyal ba'i phyir/ /dran pa dag ni kun tu spyod/ /'di yi rnam 'byor rtog pa yi/ /mtshan ma thams cad 'joms par byed/ /'di yi brtson 'grus ma lus pa/ /myur du rtoD
30a7(mdo 'grel): par bya ba'i phyir ro/ /chos kyi snang ba 'phel ba yis/ /dga' bas rtag tu rgyas par 'gyur/ /sgrib pa kun las thar ba'i phyir/ /shin tu sbyangs pas bde ba 'thob/ /ting nge 'dzin las bsams pa'i don/ /'byor ba nye bar skye bar 'gyur/ /gtang snyoms kyis ni thams
30b1(mdo 'grel): cad du/ /'di ni ji ltar 'dod bzhin gnas/ /rjes las thob dang mi rtog pa'i/ /gnas pas mchog ni rtag tu gnas/ /yon tan de lta'i sems dpa' ni/ /'khor lo sgyur ba 'dra bar 'jug/ rtag tu rin chen bdun lta bu'i/ /byang chub yan lag rnams kyis bskor/ /rang bzhin
30b2(mdo 'grel): yan lag gnas yan lag /gsum pa nges 'byung yan lag ste/ /gzhi pa phan yon yan lag yin/ /rnam gsum nyon mongs med yan lag/ de yi 'og tu ji lta bur/ /rtogs pa'i rjes su 'jug pa skye/ /rnam gzhag ji bzhin rtogs pa dang/ /rnam par bzhag
30b3(mdo 'grel): la 'jug pa dang/ /las gsum rnam par dag pa dang/ /shes bya ngag dang lam dang ni/ /yon tan khyad par can gyi ni/ /sgrib pa'i gnyen por bsgom pa'o/ /yang dag gnas pa la brten nas/ /sems la sems ni 'jog phyir dang/ /chos rab rnam par 'byed pa'i phyir//
30b4(mdo 'grel): zhi gnas dang ni lhag mthong yin/ /de ni kun 'gro cha gcig dang/ /cha gcig ma yin rgyur 'dod do/ /rtogs dang nges par 'byung ba dang/ /mtshan med 'du mi byed pa dang/ /yongs dag rnam par dag pa la/ /brten pa'i zhi gnas lhag mthong gi //rnal 'byor des kun 'gro ba
30b5(mdo 'grel): ste/ thams cad sgrub par byed pa yin/ /sangs rgyas chos rnams rdzogs bya dang/ /sems can rnams yongs smin bya dang/ /myur thob bya ba 'grub pa dang/ /las rgyun mi gcod la mkhas pa/ /byang chub sems dpa' i sa kun la/ /thabs ni mtshungs pa med pa ste/ /thabs mkhas
30b6(mdo 'grel): de la brten nas ni/ /de dag don kun sgrub bar byed/ /rnam smin thos la gomS pa dang/ /ting nge 'dzin gyi gzungs dag ni/ /chud du dang ni chen po ste/ /chen po de yang rnam pa gsum/ /blo ldan ma zhugs zhugs pa yang/ /ma dag sa pa rnams kyi ni/ /chung du dang ni 'bring bo
30b7(mdo 'grel): ste/ /dag pa'i sa pa'i gzungs chen yin/ /byang chub sems dpa' yang dang yang/ /de la yang dag brten nas ni/ /rtag tu dam pa'i chos dag kyang/ /rab tu ston zhing 'dzin pa yin/ /brtan pa rnams kyi smon lam ni/ /sems pa 'dun dang bcas pa ste/ /de ni ye shes
31a1(mdo 'grel): kyis bskul ba/ /sa rnams kun la mnyam pa med/ /de ni rgyur 'gyur shes bya ste/ /sems tsam las ni 'gyang pa'i phyir/ /sems laS mod la 'bras bu can/ /de ni ma 'ongs don grub byed/ /sna tshogs che dang byang chub par/ /sa rnams gong nas gong du mi
31a2(mdo 'grel): rnam dag byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /rang gzhan don rab sgrub byed yin/ /ting nge 'dzin gsum gyis spyod yul ni/ /bdag med rnam pa gnyis po dang/ /bdag tu 'dzin ba'i rten dang ni/ /de rtag nyer zhi yin zhes bya/ /de ni gzung 'dzin ngo bo'i phyir/ /ting 'dzin gsum du shes
31a3(mdo 'grel): par bya/ /rnam par mi rtog rgyab kyis phyogs/ /rtag tu dga' dang ldan ba'o/ /yongs su shes dang spang ba dang/ /mngon sum nyid du bya ba'i phyir/ /stong nyid la sogs ting 'dzin rnams/ /don rnams gsum du rab tu bsgrags/ /sems can rnams la phan bzhed pas/ /
31a4(mdo 'grel): nying de 'dzin gyi rgyu nyid du/ /chos kyi sdom ni rnam pa bzhi/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams la bshad/ /bstan pa rnams kyis gzhi po ni/ /med pa'i don dang rnam rtog don/ /kun tu rtog don kho na dang/ /rnam rtog nye bar zhi ba'i don/ /mi rung rgyu las skye phyir dang/ /

31b1(mdo 'grel): med gnas pa mi rung dang/ /tha ma nyid ni mi srid dang/ /sems gyi rjes su 'jug pa'i phyir/ /'dus byas thams cad skad cig ma/ /'byung ba rnams dang ngon rnam drug/ /skad cig nyid du brjod pa ni/ /skam dang 'phel dang rang bzhin gyis/ /g.yo dang 'phel dang 'grib pa'i phyir//

45a1(mdo 'grel): pa tsam las nye bar dmigs pa rtogs par byed do/ /rnam par rig pa tsam la nye bar dmigs pa las don thams cad dmigs pa med pa byed do/ /don thams cad dang med pa dang rnam pa rigs pa tsam ? ?

45a3(mdo 'grel): thams cad mi dmigs pas nye bar mtshon pa nyid kyi phyir ro/ /sbyor ba rtogs pa ni rnam pa bzhi ste/ /mos pas spyod pa'i sa la mos pas sbyor ba'i phyi dang/ /de nyid nges par 'byed pa'i gnas skabs so/ /de nyid sa dang po la so sor 'jig par
45a4(mdo 'grel): sbyor ba'i phyir dang/ de nyid ni reg pa'i gnas skabs so/ /rnam par ma dge ba'i sa drug la sgom pa la rab tu sbyor ba'i phyir dang/ /yongs su dag pa gsum po la yang ngo/ /de nyid ni rjes su dran pa'i gnas skabs so/ /sangs rgyas kyi sa la mthar phyin
45a5(mdo 'grel): pa la sbyor ba phyir te/ lhun gyis grub pas sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa gyur mi 'chad pa'i phyir ro/ /de nyid ni de'i bdag nyid ni rjes su dran pa'i gnas skabs so/ /nyes dmigs rtogs pa ni/ /gnas skabs su gyur ba med por/ /nyes dmigs rnam pa tsho'i
45a6(mdo 'grel): ste/ nyon mongs pa mi 'jug pa'i rten med pa'i nyes dmigs dang/ /lam 'jug pa'i rten med pa'i nye dmigs dang/ gang zag mya ngan las 'das par tha snyad bzhag pa ni rten med pa'i nyes dmigs pa dang/ byang chub rnam pa gsum gyi khyad par
45a7(mdo 'grel): gyi tha snyad bzhag pa'i rten med pa'i nyes dmigs so/ /de dag las bzlog pa la brten na gnas yongs su gyur ba yod pa la/ yan yon nam pa bzhi nyid du rig par bya'o/ /de rtag nyi ni gnas gyur pa ji lta ba rtogs pa rnam pa bcu rig par bya'o/ /med
45b1(mdo 'grel): pa'i chos snang ba ni/ /dper ni sgyu ma dang rmi lam la sogs pa bzhin no/ /gnas gyur pa'i dpe ni/ nam mkha' dang gser dang chu la sogs pa bzhin no// //chos dang 'od nyid rnam pa 'byed pa 'phags pa byams pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ //
45b2(mdo 'grel): rgya gar gyi mkhas po paN+Di ta shAn+ti b+ha dra dang/ zhu chen gyi lo ts+tsha ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bsgyur gyi shus te gnas la phab pa las/ slad kyi kha che'i mkhan po paN+Di ta ba ra he ta dang/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dga' rdor gyis thugs dam sa tho li shi gtsug lag khang du
45b3(mdo 'grel): bcos shing gtan la phab pa// // ` /chos dang chos nyid nang 'byed tshig bcad pa bzhugs/ /rgya gar skad du/ d+harma d+harma tA bi b+hi ga sA ri kA/ bod skad du/ chos dang chos nyid rnam par 'byed pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ mgon po byams
45b4(mdo 'grel): pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /shes nas 'ga' zhig yongs su spang bya zhing/ /gzhan 'ga' zhig ni mngon sum nyid du bya/ /des na de dag mtshan nyid rnam dbye ba/ /byed par 'dod pas bstan bcos 'di brtso bo/ /'di dag thams cad mdor bsdu na/ /rnam pa gnyis su shes bya ste/ /chos
45b5(mdo 'grel): dang de bzhin chos nyid kyis/ /thams cad bsdud pa nyid phyir ro/ /de la chos kyis phye ba ni/ /'khor ba yin te chos nyi kyis/ /rab tu phye ba theg gsum gyi/ /mya ngan las ni 'das pa'o/ /de las chos kyi mtshan nyid ni/ /gnyis dang ji lta mngon brjod par/ /snang
45b6(mdo 'grel): ba yang dag ma yin pa'i/ /kun rtog pa ste med snang phyir/ /des na yang dag ma yin pa'o/ /de yang thams cad don med cing/ /rtog tsam yin pas kun rtog pa'o/ /gzhan yang chos nyid mtshan nyid ni/ /gzung pa dang ni 'dzin pa dang/ /brjod par byang brjod par
45b7(mdo 'grel): byed/ /khyad med de bzhin nyid yin no/ /med pa snang phyir phyir 'khrul pa ni/ /kun nas nyon mongs rlu yin te/ /sgyu ma'i glang chen sro snang bzhin/ /yod pa yang ni mi snang phyir/ /med snang dar? phrag rung zhing/ /med na 'khrul dang ma 'khrul dang/ /de bzhin kun nas nyon
46a1(mdo 'grel): mongs dang/ /rnam par byed pa mi 'thad do/ /gnyis po dag ni gcig nyid dang/ /so so ba yang ma yin te/ /yod pa dang ni med pa dag /khyad par yod dang med phyir ro/ /rnam pa drug gis chos rnams la/ /'jug pa bla na med pa ste/ /bzhin nyid dang ni
46a2(mdo 'grel): grub pa ste/ /gcig dang tha dad ma yin zhing/ /gnas ni thun mong thun mong min/ /gzung dang 'dzin par snang ba ni/ /med la rab tu 'jug pas so/ /de la mtshan nyid grub pa dang/ /gcig dang tha dad ma yin la/ /ji ltar ma 'ong bstan bzhin du'o/ /gang zhig gang du 'khor
46a3(mdo 'grel): ba na/ /de ni kun tu gnas pa ste/ /sems can khams dang sdod kyi khams/ /snod kyi khams ni thun mongs ltar/ /rnam par rig pa thun mong yin/ /sems can khams ni thun mong dang/ /yang na thun mong ma yin pa'o/ /de la skye dang tha snyad dang/ /rjes su gzung dang tshar bcad
46a4(mdo 'grel): dang/ phan pa dang ni gnod pa dang/ /yon tan skyon ni phan tshun du/ /bdag po nyid kyis phan tshun du/ /yin pa'i phyir na thun med pa'o/ /gnas dang rnam par rig pa dang/ /bde sdug las dang 'chi'i 'pho dang/ /skye ba dang ni bcangs pa dang/ /grol 'thun mong ma yin phyir/ /de nas thun mong ma yin
46a5(mdo 'grel): pa'o/ /phyi rol bzung ba thun mong bar/ /snang ba 'dzin pa'i rnam rig pa'o/ /rnam par shes las phyi rol tu/ /gyur ba'i don yod ma yin te/ /thun mong ba nyid yin phyir ro/ /chig shos thun mong ma yin pa'i/ /bzung ba rnam par rig pa'i don/ /gzhan
46a6(mdo 'grel): gyi sems la sogs pa ni/ /mnyam par ma bzhag mnyam bzhag pa'i/ /'dzin pa'i rnam par rig pa la/ /phan tshun yul gyur ma yin te/ /mnyam pa ma bzhag pa la ni/ /rang gi rnam rtog snang phyir dang/ /mnyam par bzhag pa dag la ni/ /ting nge 'dzin gyi
46a7(mdo 'grel): spyod yul de'i/ /gzugs brnyan rab tu snang phyir ro/ /bzung bar snang ba med grub na/ /'dzin par snang ba med grub bo/ /de la kyang ni bzung ba dang/ /'dzin par snang ba med pa la/ /'jug pa grub ste thog med pa'i/ /kun nas ldang ba grub pas so/ /
46b1(mdo 'grel): gnyis su yongs su 'grub par/ /rab tu grub par yin phyir ro/ /rnam pa drug gis chos nyid la/ /'jug pa bla na med pa ste/ /mtshan nyid kun tu gnas pa dang/ /nges par 'byed dang reg pa dang/ /rjes su dran dang de dag nyid/ /nye bar son la 'jug pas so/ /mtshan nyid
46b2(mdo 'grel): mdo ni ji lta bzhin/ /gnas ni chos rnams thams cad de/ /'on kyang mdo sde thams cad kyang/ /de la nges par 'byed pa ni/ /theg pa chen po'i mdo sde la/ /brten pa'i tshul bzhin yid byed pas/ /bsdus pa'i sbyor lam thams cad do/ /reg pa yang dag lta thob phyir//
46b3(mdo 'grel): mthong pa'i lam gyis mngon sum gyi/ /tshul du de bzhin nyid thob cing/ /nyams su myong ba gang yin pa'o/ /rjes su dran pa reg pas ni/ /mthong ba'i don la sgom lam gyi/ /byang chub phyogs kyis bsdus pa te/ /de yi dri ma sel ba'i phyir/ /de la de yi bdag nyid
46b4(mdo 'grel): du/ /nye bar son pa de bzhin nyid/ /dri ma med par gyur pa na/ /thams cad de bzhin nyid tsam du/ /snang ba de yang gnas gyur pa/ /grub pa yin no rnam pa bcus/ /gnas yod gyur la 'jug pa ni/ /bla na med pa nyid yin te/ /ngo bo rdzas dang gang
46b5(mdo 'grel): zag dang/ /khyad par dgos pa gnas dang ni/ /yid la byed dang sbyor ba dang/ /nyes dmigs phan yon 'jug pas so/ /de la ngo bo 'jug pa ni/ /blo bur ba yi dri ma dang/ /de bzhin nyid ni snang ba dang/ /snang ba'i don te de bzhin nyid/ /dri ma med pa gang
46b6(mdo 'grel): yin pa'o/ /dngos po rdzas su 'jug pa ni/ /thun mong snod kyi rnam rig pa/ /de bzhin nyid du gyur pa dang/ /mdo sde chos kyi dbyings nyid kyi/ /de bzhin nyid du gyur ba dang/ /thun mong min pa sems can gyi/ /khams kyi rnam par rig pa yi/ /de
46b7(mdo 'grel): bzhin nyid du gyur pa'o/ /gang zag dag la 'jug pa ni/ /dang po gnyis ni sangs rgyas dang/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi na/ /de bzhin nyid yongs gyur pa ste/ /phyi ma nyan thos rnams dang ni/ /rang sangs rgyas kyi yang yin no/ /khyad bar
47a1(mdo 'grel): can la 'jug pa ni/ /sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ /zhing yongs su dag pa'i khyad par dang/ /chos sku longs spyod rdzogs pa dang/ /sprul sku thob pas gzigs pa dang/ /'doms pa dang mi tsang? 'byor nyid/ /thob pa'i
47a2(mdo 'grel): khyad par las yin no/ /dgos pa rtogs la 'jug pa ni/ /sngon gyi smon lam khyad par dang/ /theg pa chen pos ston pa yis/ /dmigs pa'i khyad par ma bcu la/ /rab tu sbyor ba'i khyad par ro/ /gnas sam rten la 'jug pa ni/ /rnam par mi rtogs ye shes
47a3(mdo 'grel): la/ /'jug pa rnam pa drug gis te/ /dmigs dang mtshan ma spangs pa dang/ /yang dag pa yis sbyor ba dang/ /mtshan nyid dang ni phan yon dang/ /yongs su shes la 'jug pas so/ /de la dang po dmigs pa la/ /'jug pa rnam bzhir shes pa bya ste/

49b8(mdo 'grel): par dbye ba med chos phyir/ /lhun grub rnam par mi rtogs phyir/ /rtogs bya rtogs pa de yi ni/ /yan lag rtogs par byed phyir te/ /go rim ji bzhin gnas gcig ste/ /dag rgyu gsum ni rkyen yin no/ /rdzogs sangs sku ni 'phro phyir dang/ /de bzhin

50a2(mdo 'grel): don dam dbyings kyi dgongs don yin shes bya/ /rin chen nam mkha' chu dag bzhin/ /rtag tu rang bzhin nyon mongs med/ /chos mos lhag pa'i shes rab dang/ /ting 'dzin snying rje las byung ba/ /mthu dang gzhan du mi 'gyur dang/ /brlan pa'i ngo
50a3(mdo 'grel): bo rang bzhin phyir/ /'di dag nor bu rin chen mkha' / /chu yi yon tan chos mthun nyid/ /chos la khong khro bdag lta dang/ /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal gyis 'jigs dang/ /sems can don la ltos med nyid/ /'dod chen mu stegs nyan thos dang//
50a4(mdo 'grel): rang 'byung rnams kyi sgrib rnam bzhi/ /dag rgyu lhag par smos pa las/ /sogs pa'i chos ni rnam bzhi nyid/ /theg mchog la mos sa bon shes rab ni/ /sangs rgyas chos bskyed ma dang bsam gtan gyi/ /bde ba mngal gnas snying rje'i ma ma can//
50a5(mdo 'grel): gang yin de dag thub pa'i rjes skyes sras/ /gtsang bdag bde dang rtag nyid kyi/ /yon tan pha rol tu phyin 'bras/ /sdug bsngal yid 'byung zhi thob par/ /'dun dang smon pa'i las can no/ /'di dag 'dras ni mdor bsdu na/ /chos kyi sku la
50a6(mdo 'grel): phyin ci log /rnam pa bzhi las bzlog pa yi/ /gnyen pos rab tu phye ba nyid/ /de ni rang bzhin dag phyir dang/ /bag chags spangs phyir gtsang ba yin/ /bag dang bdag med spros pa dag /nye bar zhi bas dam pa'i bdag /yid kyi rang

50b1(mdo 'grel): bsten nas/ /'phags pa 'khor ba'am mya ngan 'da' mi 'gyur/ /gal te sangs rgyas khams med na/ /sdug la skyo bar mi 'gyur zhing/ /mya ngan 'das la 'dod pa dang/ /don gnyer smon pa 'ang med par 'gyur/ /srid dang mya ngan 'das pa de'i/ /sdug
50b2(mdo 'grel): bde'i skyon yon mthong ba 'di/ /rigs yod las yin gang phyir de/ /rigs med dag la med phyir ro/ /rgya mtsho che bzhin dpag med pa/ /yon tan rin chen mi zad gnas/ /dbyer med yon tan dang ldan pa'i/ /ngo bo nyid phyir mar me bzhin/ /chos
50b3(mdo 'grel): sku rgyal ba'i ye shes dang/ /thugs rje'i khams ni bsdus pa'i phyir/ /snod dang rin chen chu yis 'di/ /rgya mtsho dang ni mtshungs par bstan/ /dri med gnas la mngon shes dang/ /ye shes dri med de nyid dang/ /rnam dbye med phyir mar ma yi//
50b4(mdo 'grel): snang dang dro 'dog chos mtshungs can/ /so so'i skye 'phags rdzogs sangs kyi/ /de bzhin nyid dbye'i 'jug pa las/ /de nyid gzigs pas sems can la/ /rgyal ba'i snying po 'di bstan to/ /so so'i? skye bo phyin ci log /bden pa mthong ba bzlog
50b5(mdo 'grel): pa ste/ /de bzhin gshegs pa ji lta bzhin/ /phyin ci ma log spros med nyid/ /ma dag ma dag dag pa dang/ /shin tu rnam dag go rim bzhin/ /sems can byang chub sems dpa' dang/ /de bzhin gshegs pa zhes brjod do/ /ngo bo nyid

50b7(mdo 'grel): dbyings/ /de bzhin kun tu 'gro ba nyid/ /de spyi'i mtshan nyid nyes pa dang/ /yon tan mthar thug khyab pa ste/ /gzugs kyi rnam pa dman pa dang/ /bar ma mchog la nam mkha' bzhin/ /nyes pa glo bur dang ldan dang/ /yon tan rang bzhin nyid
51a1(mdo 'grel): ldan phyir/ /ji ltar sngar bzhin phyis de bzhin/ /'gyur ba med pa'i chos nyid do/ /ji ltar nam mkha' kun song ba/ /phra zhing nye bar gos pa med/ /de bzhin sems can thams cad la/ /gnas 'di nye bar gos pa med/ /de
51a2(mdo 'grel): ltar 'jig rten thams cad du/ /nam mkha' las ni skye zhing 'jig /de bzhin 'dus ma byas dbyings la/ /dbang po rnams ni skye zhing 'jig /ji ltar nam mkha' me rnams kyis/ /sngon chad nam yang tshigs pa med/ /de bzhin 'di ni 'chi ba dang//
51a3(mdo 'grel): na dang brga ba'i mes ma 'chi ba/ /sa ni chu la chu rlung la/ /rlung ni mkha' la rab tu gnas/ /mkha' ni rlung dang chu dag dang/ /sa yi khams la gnas ma yin/ /de bzhin phung po khams dbang rnams/ las dang nyon mongs dag la gnas//
51a4(mdo 'grel): las dang nyon mongs tshul bzhin min/ /yid la byed la rtog tu gnas/ /tshul bzhin ma yin yid byed ni/ /sems kyi dag pa la rab gnas/ /sems kyi rang bzhin chos rnams ni/ /thams cad la yang gnas pa med/ /sa dang 'dra bar phung
51a5(mdo 'grel): po dang/ /skye mched khams rnams shes bar bya/ /chu khams dang 'dra lus can gyi/ /las dang nyon mongs shes bya ste/ /tshul bzhin ma yin yid byed ni/ /rlung gi khams dang 'dra bar blta/ /rang bzhin mkha' i khams bzhin du/ /de bzhin

51a7(mdo 'grel): de 'jigs pa dang chags pa dang/ /skye dang 'jig par 'gyur ba yin/ /sems kyi rang bzhin nam mkha' yi/ /khams ltas? rgyu med rkyen med de/ /tshogs pa med cing skye ba dang/ /'jig pa gnas pa'ang yong ma yin/ /sems kyi rang bzhin 'od
51b1(mdo 'grel): gsal gang yin pa/ /de ni nam mkha' bzhin du 'gyur med de/ /yang dag ming rtog las byung 'dod chags sogs/ /glo bur dri mas de nyon mongs mi 'gyur/ /las dang nyon mongs chu tshogs kyis/ /'di ni mngon par 'grub min te/ /'chi dang na dang rgal
51b2(mdo 'grel): med/ /mi bzad pas kyang tshig mi 'gyur/ /dus mdza' dmyal ba tha mal pa'i/ /me gsum mchi dang na ba dang/ /rga ba'i me gsum rim bzhin du/ /de dang 'dra bar shes par bya/ /skye mchi na dang rga ba las grol ba/ /'di yi rang bzhin ji bzhin nyid rtogs

51b4(mdo 'grel): mthong ba'i phyir/ /skye sogs rnams laS 'das gyur kyang/ /snying rje'i bdag nyid skye ba dang/ /'chi dang rga dang na bar ston/ /rgyal sras 'gyur med chos nyid 'di/ /rtogs na ma rigs ldongs rnam kyi/ /skye ba la sogs dag tu ni/ /mthong ba gang
51b5(mdo 'grel): yin te smad do/ /'phags pa'i spyod yul thob pa gang/ /byis pa'i spyod yul du ston te/ /de nyid phyir na 'gro ba yi/ /gnyen gyis thabs dang snying rje'i mchog /de ni 'jig rten thams cad las/ /'das kyang 'jig rten las ma g.yos/ /'jig
51b6(mdo 'grel): rten don du 'jig rten na/ /'jig rten dri mas ma gos spyod/ /ji ltar pad+ma chu nang du/ /skyes pa chu yis gos pa med/ /de bzhin 'di ni 'jig rten du/ /skyes kyang 'jig rten chos mi gos/ /bya ba sgrub la rtag tu blo/ /mi bzhin du ni 'bar
51b7(mdo 'grel): ba dang/ /zhi ba'i bsam gtan snyoms 'jug la/ /rtag tu snyoms par 'jugs pa yin/ /sngon gyi 'phen pa'i dbang dang ni/ /rnam rtog thams cad bral ba'i phyir/ /de ni lus can smin pa yi/ /don du 'bad pa byed ma yin/ /bstan dang gzugs
52a1(mdo 'grel): sku dag dang ni/ /spyod dang spyod lam gyis kyang rung/ /gang zhig ji ltar gang gis 'dul/ /des de de ltar nyid du shes/ /de ltar nam mkha' i mdza' klas kyis/ /'gro ba rtag tu lhun grub par/ /thogs med blo ldan de yin ni//

52a3(mdo 'grel): kyis /khyad par gang yin sangs rgyas dang/ /byang chub sems dpa' i khyad de nyid/ /gzhan 'gyur min bdag mi zad chos ldan phyir/ /'gro skyabs phyi ma'i mdza' med mur thugs phyir/ /de ni rtag tu gnyis med mi rtog phyir/ /'jig med chos

55a4(mdo 'grel): yin par brjod/ /chags dang sdang dang rmongs dang de'i/ /kun dang drag dang bag chags dang/ /mthong sgom lam spangs ma dag dang/ /dag pa'i sa la brten pa yi/ /dri ma rnam dgu pad+ma yi/ /sbubs sogs dpes?
